1a1(phal chen): (nga) @#/ ! /sangs rgyas phal po che bzhugs so/ /
1a2(phal chen): (黃) 大方廣佛華嚴經第四部
1b1(phal chen): bam po dang po/ dum bu bzhi pa/ de nas byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs chen po de'i nang nas byang chub sems
1b2(phal chen): dpa' kha cig 'di snyam du sems te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ni ci
1b3(phal chen): tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang 'byung
1b4(phal chen): ba rnam par dag pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis myi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin
1b5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sku gdung ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis myi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
1b6(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas skye ba ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis myi khyab pa/ sangs rgyas bcom
1b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis myi khyab/
2a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ni ji tsam zhig du
2a2(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis myi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa myi
2a3(phal chen): mnga' ba'i rnam par spyod pa ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab snyam pa dang / de nas
2a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi sems mkhyen pas thugs su chud nas/ byang chub sems dpa' ud pa la'i snying po/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis byin du brlabs
2a5(phal chen): so/ /sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis byin dang ldan par mdzad do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis snang ba mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis yongs su rgyas par mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi myi
2a6(phal chen): 'jigs pa la rab tu bzhag go/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa khong du chud par mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do/ /chags
2a7(phal chen): pa myed pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go/ /sangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs par mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod du med pa la rab tu
2a8(phal chen): gzhag pa mdzad do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' ud pa la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa rig cing khong du chud pas chags pa med pa'i dbyings su sgrub pa'i yid dang / chos thams cad la sgrib pa med
2b1(phal chen): par gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i sangs rgyas blta ba dang / snying pos lta ba'i sems can thams
2b2(phal chen): cad yongs su sbyong ba'i go ca chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyun chad pa myed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa skad cig gi cha shas la rnam par spyod pa dang /
2b3(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo mthong ba mi zad pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i rnam pa gzungs thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' pad mo'i snying po la 'di
2b4(phal chen): skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul ba chen po la rnam
2b5(phal chen): par spyod pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la/ sku'i mtshan thams cad rab tu brnyes pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi 'khor lo
2b6(phal chen): bskor ba ni ting nge 'dzin dang / dgongs pas sbyar ba'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi ni brjod du med pa yang brjod du shin tu bstan pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan
2b7(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab par spyod pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas
2b8(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa ni brjod du myed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ni thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'o/ /kye rgyal
3a1(phal chen): ba'i sras dag / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud cing / bstan pa ni sgrib pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bcu po 'di dag ni
3a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku gzugs kyi rnam par dag pa ni
3a3(phal chen): rnyog pa med par rgyud thams cad du byung bas mtha' dang dbus myed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i spyan ni chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang
3a4(phal chen): dbus myed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i snyan ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgra sgrib pa med par thugs su chud pas mtha' dang dbus myed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
3a5(phal chen): shangs kyi skye mched ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dbus myed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni sangs rgyas kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes
3a6(phal chen): pas mtha' dang dbus myed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljags shin tu yangs pa ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gsung gi dbyangs rjes su 'gro bas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan
3a7(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sku'i chos nyid ni sems can thams cad ma lus pa'i sems kyi rnam pa la de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba rnam par dmyigs pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
3a8(phal chen): rnams kyi sku dang tha myi dad cing dus gsum chags pa med par thugs su chud cing shes pa dang rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa
3b1(phal chen): sgrib pa mi mnga' ba la rnam par spyod pa ni sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang dang rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi
3b2(phal chen): khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni brjod du med pa'i rgyan byin gyis brlabs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang dag par bstan te/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmyigs par mdzad pas
3b3(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa ni rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos yongs su rdzogs te/
3b4(phal chen): chos thams cad rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dbus med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus myed
3b5(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par sgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o/ /bcu gang zhe na/ skad cig
3b6(phal chen): gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i tshe yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig
3b7(phal chen): la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs shing mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su bstan pa
3b8(phal chen): dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su smin
4a1(phal chen): pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du/ dus la bab pa shes pas sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sems can ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du
4a2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmyigs pa yongs su bstan pa dang skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/ rgyan sna tshogs dang rgyan brjod du med
4a3(phal chen): pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par dag pa gcig ma yin pa
4a4(phal chen): thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad du dbang po dang / brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dad pa
4a5(phal chen): byung ba dang / mos pa dang / spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba las dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyud mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su bstan pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
4a6(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da'
4a7(phal chen): ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam par smin pa dang /
4a8(phal chen): rnam par smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa yongs su smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams
4b1(phal chen): lung bstan pa ni de'i dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud du/ cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus la mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs
4b2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongs su bstan pa de ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
4b3(phal chen): btang snyoms su bzhugs pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang / grong dang / grong brdal du gshegs pa de ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab
4b4(phal chen): pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongs su 'dzin pa na/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
4b5(phal chen): rnams sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
4b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ rnam par 'phrul ba bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
4b7(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/
4b8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skyil mo krung gcig gis rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus cig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / 'od gzer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa
5a1(phal chen): thams cad snang bar bya ba dang / sku gzugs gcig gis lus dang / gzugs thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus
5a2(phal chen): par byon pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye shes gcig rtogs pas chos thams cad la sgrib pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang /
5a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad myed pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gis rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / 'gro ba
5a4(phal chen): thams cad dang ma 'dres par bzhugs shing 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / myi dmyigs pa'i tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gcig pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i
5a5(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe myed cing bsam gyis myi khyab pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas
5a6(phal chen): kyi byin gyis brlab mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jug pa myed pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas/ smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par
5a7(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad myi gnyis pa la mngon par 'tshang rgya ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems can gyi mthar thug par bdag myed pa la sems can 'dul bar mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /
5a8(phal chen): chos thams cad mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'du ba dang / 'jig pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul thams
5b1(phal chen): cad mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la/ las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa la/ chos kyi dbyings su gsung mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams
5b2(phal chen): cad kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa la skye ba dang / 'jig rten pa'i
5b3(phal chen): mtshan nyid rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs
5b4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs su chud pa dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku ni dus gsum thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i khongs su chud pa yin/
5b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa ni/ cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas
5b6(phal chen): pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi'i
5b7(phal chen): khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad yongs su myi gtong ba ni thugs rje chen po'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rtag tu mnyam par
5b8(phal chen): gzhag pa ni dus thams cad du sems can thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba ni sems can rnam par 'dul ba thams cad khongs
6a1(phal chen): su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad khongs du chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi skad cig
6a2(phal chen): gcig tu ni 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nyi ma gcig tu ni dus gsum gyi bskal pa'i
6a3(phal chen): grangs khong du chud par bstan pa thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs su chud pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu
6a4(phal chen): po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma rab tu 'joms zhing rnam par 'thor ba ni sangs rgyas
6a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /mu stegs can gzhan dang phas kyi rgol ba tshar gcad pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos
6a6(phal chen): bzod par dka' ba'o/ /'dul ba'i sems can thams cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /sems can
6a7(phal chen): 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad tu gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa'i ye shes ni sangs rgyas
6a8(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skus khyab cing sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par phye ba sna tshogs thams cad du/
6b1(phal chen): mi gnyis pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /gsung gi yan lag thams cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang / thos par bya ba dang /
6b2(phal chen): gdul bar bya ba don yod par yang dag par rig pa thogs pa myed pas bstan pa'i tshul du so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi 'byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos
6b3(phal chen): bzod par dka' ba'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi ba spu'i bu ga gcig nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bsam gyis mi khyab cing /
6b4(phal chen): thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni sangs rgyas bcom
6b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig
6b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongs su ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang rang bzhin gyi lhab lhub dang / chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing sems can rnam par
6b7(phal chen): 'dul ba thogs pa med pa la 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang mi bde ba dang / gnod pa med kyang rdul shin tu phra ba de'ang yangs par ma byas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chung bar
6b8(phal chen): ma byas par ji ltar gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mnga' ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /mun pa med pa'i
7a1(phal chen): khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing sgrib pa mi mnga' la sems can pha rol kyi sgrib pa sna tshogs kyi gnas rnam par
7a2(phal chen): sel na/ de la de bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
7a3(phal chen): de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba rnam
7a4(phal chen): pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag par sgrubs pa bdag nyid che ba ni sngon gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du kha
7a5(phal chen): na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de
7a6(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam par dag pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa ste/
7a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par gnas pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing / shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas
7a8(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus gsum la mi gnas par rnam par spyod cing chos thams cad la rten par yang dag par dgra bcom pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa
7b1(phal chen): thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa la rnam par gzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
7b2(phal chen): rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas/
7b3(phal chen): mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin du rnam par
7b4(phal chen): dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang kha dog mtha' yas pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par bzhugs
7b5(phal chen): pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi brnyes
7b6(phal chen): pas bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar bzhugs shing / khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ro 'byin te rgol ba'i nang na stag lta bu mthu dang ldan pa la chos thams cad bstan pa la thugs sgron ma lta bu mnga' bas/
7b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las
7b8(phal chen): 'das nas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang mtshan kyi tshig thos pa tsam gyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems can rnams kyi yon shin tu sbyong zhing mya ngan las 'das nas/ de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon tan zad par mi 'gyur bas/
8a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba
8a2(phal chen): med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs shing 'jig rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na bzhugs
8a3(phal chen): kyang 'jig rten gyi khams 'di sems can rnams kyis rjes su dran par byas nas sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha
8a4(phal chen): na ma tho ba myed cing shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba
8a5(phal chen): med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
8a6(phal chen): 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag pa la sngon gyi smon lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i
8a7(phal chen): tshul khrim kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa sel bas shin tu rnams par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
8a8(phal chen): rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnams par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rigs
8b1(phal chen): rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang / dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas
8b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi sku rnyog pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po sgrib pa med pas shin tu rnam
8b3(phal chen): par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa thams cad la mthu chen po bsnyes shing / pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu rnam par dag pa
8b4(phal chen): yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad
8b5(phal chen): pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa thob pa'i sems can rnams la dus thams cad du sangs rgyas bstan pa
8b6(phal chen): dang / sems can sems cang shes dang ldan pa rnams la/ dus thams cad du chos bstan pa dang / sems can sangs rgyas la dad pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dus thams cad du bskyed pa dang / chos
8b7(phal chen): kyang skyon med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa dus thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / de bzhin
8b8(phal chen): gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dus thams cad du/ chags pa mi mnga' bar gshegs pa dang / sems can thams cad la thugs rje chen po dus thams cad du myi gtong
9a1(phal chen): ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par
9a2(phal chen): 'phrul pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad du 'byung ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
9a3(phal chen): bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gnas pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
9a4(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku ye shes rgya
9a5(phal chen): mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med pa brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs
9a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi spyan gyi yu la mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /
9a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi char mngon par 'bab pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan legs pa mang po
9a8(phal chen): mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha'i mur thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyad par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/
9b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par sgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
9b2(phal chen): ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi
9b3(phal chen): non pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i
9b4(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba 'di ni sangs
9b5(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste chos
9b6(phal chen): thams cad kyang thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste thams cad kyang stobs bcu tshad med pa dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
9b7(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste thams cad kyang
9b8(phal chen): sems can 'dul ba la yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni
10a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
10a2(phal chen): kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste mi gnyis par yang dag par spyod pa'i mtshan nyid kyis chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no/ /'di lta ste ji ltar
10a3(phal chen): yongs su smin par 'gyur ba dang / dul bar 'gyur pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi yul mu med pas sangs rgyas kyi yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi tshul yin te/ kye rgyal
10a4(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul lo/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos mtha' yas pa
10a5(phal chen): shin tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom
10a6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par
10a7(phal chen): smin pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams ngag dang man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas
10a8(phal chen): pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can mtha' yas pa rnam par spyod pa'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub
10b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams ngag dang man ngag gis yongs su gzhol ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' khyad par
10b2(phal chen): gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang 'jig pa
10b3(phal chen): shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su bstan
10b4(phal chen): pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas
10b5(phal chen): gcig tu brgyud pa ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongs su bshad pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/
10b6(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas
10b7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la bsgrub pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongs su bstan pa ni sems
10b8(phal chen): can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /sangs rgyas
11a1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mang ba yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa yang sems can
11a2(phal chen): rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /sa dang chu dang mye dang / rlung gis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /
11a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin kyis brlabs kyi yul dang mi dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /sangs
11a4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zhing la dmyigs par mdzad pas kyang sems
11a5(phal chen): can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin
11a6(phal chen): las bsgrub po/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams myi gsung bar bzhugs pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
11a7(phal chen): de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la bsgrub pa'o/ / //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po gnyis pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom
11a8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos te/ bcu gang zhe na/ smon lam chen po la rab tu brten zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de ltar mdzad cing gnyis su
11b1(phal chen): mi gsung ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dang po'o/ /phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pas
11b2(phal chen): rab tu brtson zhing sgyid lug pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o/ /sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba gcig gcig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
11b3(phal chen): med par gshegs shing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa la thag thogs med pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gsum pa'o/ /zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos
11b4(phal chen): snyoms pa dang / dad pa'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bzhi pa'o/ /gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs
11b5(phal chen): nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su mi 'gyur ro/ /snyam du byang chub
11b6(phal chen): kyi sems ma nyams pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos lnga pa'o/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsgrub cing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo bas 'jug gi/ 'jig rten
11b7(phal chen): pa'i rgyud la ma yin pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos drug pa'o/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su sngon sangs rgyas gyis spyad pa'i sems su lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid
11b8(phal chen): kyi las kyis slob cing nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo ba med pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa
12a1(phal chen): 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing 'od gsal ba dang / thams cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos
12a2(phal chen): thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o/ /'jig rten pa'i bde ba thams cad yongs su
12a3(phal chen): spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis gos pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis/ 'jig rten thams cad bde ba thams
12a4(phal chen): cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang spros pa thams cad rab tu 'joms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o/ /sdug bsngal gyi myi bde ba thams cad nyams su bab ste/ 'gro
12a5(phal chen): ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub gyis shin tu gdungs kyang bla bar sems bskyed pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs kyi nges su srung ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu'i bar du sangs rgyas
12a6(phal chen): kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so/ /
12a7(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
12a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na
12b1(phal chen): bzhugs pa myi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa dang bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pa chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par
12b2(phal chen): spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pa chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
12b3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa
12b4(phal chen): thams cad ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa
12b5(phal chen): thams cad tsam kyi 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa la
12b6(phal chen): gzigs shing / thugs kyi skad gcig cig la cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis sems can rnam par 'dul yang chags pa myi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
12b7(phal chen): rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad myed pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa myi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
12b8(phal chen): l dan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis myi khyab par ston cing
13a1(phal chen): gsung yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med
13a2(phal chen): pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku
13a3(phal chen): mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyis rnam par brgyan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
13a4(phal chen): gsung yan lag gi mchog dam pa drug bcu dang ldan zhing yan lag lnga brgyas yongs su bzung ba dang / rgyan brgya stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' yas mu med pas
13a5(phal chen): rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi don dang tshig dang yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim par mdzad pa dang / bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar seng ge'i nga ro chen po sgrogs pa dang /
13a6(phal chen): 'jigs pa myed pa chen pos bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sems can thams cad la grag cing stsal te/ khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sems can
13a7(phal chen): bsam pa tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha dad pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar nye bar gnas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
13a8(phal chen): r nams kyi thugs kyi phrin las ni stobs bcus brgyan pa sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin chen po thams cad kyi me tog shin tu rgyas pa sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan cing sgrubs
13b1(phal chen): pas chags pa med pa'i spyod yul dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab tu brnyes pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur
13b2(phal chen): pa/ dus gsum kyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs
13b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed par mdzad de/ 'od zer
13b4(phal chen): de dag re re la yang 'od zer gyi 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byed cing 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med
13b5(phal chen): par ston pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba dang mi 'bral bas/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pas gnas pa med pa rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung
13b6(phal chen): ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzhad mo 'dzum par ston na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od
13b7(phal chen): z er kha dog sna tshogs kha dog du ma dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa sems can gyi khams tshad
13b8(phal chen): med grangs med bsam gyi myi khyab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lung ston pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du shin tu gsal bar 'byung ste/
14a1(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis zhal 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/
14a2(phal chen): sgrib pa med pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad la chags pa med pa nyid kyis mthar thug pa mtha' dang dbus med pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa 'jig rten
14a3(phal chen): thams cad dang 'dre ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las 'das pa'i chos kyis
14a4(phal chen): yang dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang khams dang / skye mched bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku'i rgyan
14a5(phal chen): mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'od ma 'dres shing / rgyan du ma dang ldan pa kha
14a6(phal chen): dog sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i 'od kyi snang ba kun tu thogs pa med cing / thams cad du chags pa med pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sgrib pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzod du
14a7(phal chen): gyur pa/ 'od thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog mtha'
14a8(phal chen): yas pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog yid du 'ong ba mnga' ba'o/ /kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga' ba'o/ /kha dog tshad med pa mnga' ba'o/ /sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / mos pa bzhin du rnam par dmigs pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o/ /
14b1(phal chen): de ma yin pa'i kha dog gzhan khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o/ /kha dog thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
14b2(phal chen): ni kha dog bla na med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin tu rnam
14b3(phal chen): par dag pa ste/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o/ /chos nyid kyi rnam pa thams
14b4(phal chen): cad du khyad par yod pa dang khyad par med pa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes skye ba thams cad kyi nang du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs sgrib pa med pa'i rgyud rnam
14b5(phal chen): par dag pas/ 'jig rten gyi mi snyan pa thams cad kyis mi snyan par brjod du med pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / rgyud rnam par dag pa'i
14b6(phal chen): rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po'i mthu dang rang bzhin gyi rgyan mnga' ba ste/ shin tu dang bas yongs su rtog pa'i rnyog pa myi
14b7(phal chen): mnga' ba sku'i phrin las yongs su bstsal ba lta bas mi skyo ba/ dgongs pa shin tu rnam par bstsal ba thugs rje chen po mnga' ba/ 'gro ba thams cad skyob pa yon gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med
14b8(phal chen): pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtse ba can phan par mdzad pa sems can thams cad kyi don tu ye shes chen po byin gyis brlabs te/ bsod nams chen pos yongs su 'phags pa 'gro
15a1(phal chen): ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang / ye shes kyi phung po thams cad rnam par 'phel bar mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
15a2(phal chen): rnams kyi byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bsod nams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
15a3(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos rnams te/
15a4(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad la snang bar mdzad pa'i mnga' bsgyur bas/ tshig dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la thogs pa mi
15a5(phal chen): mnga' ba'i spobs pa mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad ma lus par yongs su brjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur
15a6(phal chen): ba'i chos dang po'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ji ltar yongs su smin pa dang / smon lam ji ltar btab pa'i tshul bzhin du/ 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' bas mnga' che ba
15a7(phal chen): ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos gnyis pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad sems can gcig la yang gnod pa
15a8(phal chen): med par rnam pa drug du rab tu bskyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyan rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshad med pa dang ldan pa nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu 'phang ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bzhug pa dang /
15b1(phal chen): gcig nas gcig tu bsdu ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsre bas 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang gzhan dag gzhan gyi phyogs su rab tu bzhag kyang sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor zhing rmongs par
15b2(phal chen): mi 'gyur la/ the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos gsum pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig
15b3(phal chen): rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis brlob pa'i ye shes kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan phan tshun du byin gyis brlab pa dang / dgongs pa'i skad gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams
15b4(phal chen): thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa dang / bskal ba grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams cad
15b5(phal chen): kyis rnam par brgyan pa dang / mi mthun pa med cing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu yongs su 'du bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa thams cad byin
15b6(phal chen): gyis brlabs pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos bzhi pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan
15b7(phal chen): ' das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can gzigs na sems can gcig gi don du bskal ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs na yang
15b8(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la myi bde ba mi mnga' zhing thugs la mi bde ba myi mnga' ste/ gang zag de yang mi snyel bas 'dul ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang /
16a1(phal chen): gang zag gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du rim pa rim pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad
16a2(phal chen): du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i sku tshe la mnga' bar byin kyis brlab te bzhugs kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyo ba mi mnga' ste/ de ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad
16a3(phal chen): mthar gyis rim pas sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang zag gi don du yongs su bskyod par mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i
16a4(phal chen): chos lnga pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du yang dag par gzhol ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa bzhud pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams
16a5(phal chen): cad du bzhud pa la thag thogs mi mnga' ba dang / phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud thams
16a6(phal chen): cad du dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i bzhud par byin gyis brlob cing / chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa khong du chud par bya bas chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med pa rab tu bskor ba la mnga'
16a7(phal chen): che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos drug pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi
16a8(phal chen): khams thams cad kyi don du dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar mnga' che ba ste/ de la chos thams cad mngon
16b1(phal chen): par sangs rgyas pa gang yang med la/ gang mngon par sangs rgyas pa gang yang med la/ gang gis mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'ang med de/ mngon par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba med kyang slob
16b2(phal chen): pa'i sa la gnas shing / mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang sgrib pa med par rtogs par thugs su chud pas/ sems can thams cad
16b3(phal chen): gdul ba'i don du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongs su rgyun mi gcod pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga'
16b4(phal chen): chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos bdun pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyan gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de snyan gyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do/ /
16b5(phal chen): snyan gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de shangs kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do/ /shangs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de ljags
16b6(phal chen): ljags kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do/ /ljags kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de ni sku'i skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do/ /sku'i skye
16b7(phal chen): mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de thugs kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do/ /thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi khams
17a1(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad kyi dmigs pa 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa sna tshogs rnam par phye ba thams cad grub par mdzad do/ /de bzhin du dmigs pa thams cad re re yang snrel bzhir
17a2(phal chen): bsgrub pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos brgyad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rang gi
17a3(phal chen): sku'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig gi nang du sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzud pa mdzad cing khongs su chud par mdzad pa dang / sems can re re zhing yang lus sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa tsam du
17a4(phal chen): yangs par mdzad kyang sems can de dag la gnod par mi 'gyur ba dang / de dag du yang sems can re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams gcig tu brgyud pas bskal pa grangs med pa zad par gnas par bya ba dang /
17a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gom pa gcig gis phyin pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu sangs rgyas byung ba rnams kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas de dag byung ba'i tshe yang brjod du
17a6(phal chen): med pa'i 'jig rten gyis khams gyi rgyud dang / gling de dag na sems can gyi gtso bo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bya ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga de nas sangs rgyas gcig nas
17a7(phal chen): gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa
17a8(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings bstan pa gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan par bya ba dang / 'das pa gcig nas gcig tu
17b1(phal chen): brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / da ltar byung ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa yongs su brjod par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang
17b2(phal chen): dbus med par bstan pa kun tu mtshams med par sems can thams cad 'ong zhing 'gro ba dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du 'dod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen po gegs med pa thams cad 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/
17b3(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos dgu pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad pad mos brgyan pa'i seng
17b4(phal chen): ge'i khri pad mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa thams cad du khyab pa'i skus byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams
17b5(phal chen): cad yongs su bstan par mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gis ji lta bar 'jig rten gyi khams sems can kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sems can gyi gtso bo thams cad kyang de bzhin du dgongs
17b6(phal chen): pa skad cig ma re re'i byin gyi rlabs kyis brlab pa dang / dgongs pa skad cig la ji lta ba de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma thams cad la yang / pad mo'i rgyud kyis yongs su dag par mngon par 'tshang
17b7(phal chen): rgya bar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa rnam par dag pa/ rgyan sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dmigs pa rnam pa
17b8(phal chen): sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa 'byam klas pa/ brjod du med pa mtshan nyid tha dad pa rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyud tshad med cing 'byam klas pa/ dus kyi rgyud grangs med pa dang ldan pa
18a1(phal chen): bstan pa ma 'dres pa dang ldan pa/ blo tshad med pa dang mos pa shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pa/ mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ tshad med pa thams
18a2(phal chen): cad dgongs pa skad cig ma las dgongs pa skad gcig ma gcig gis thams cad yongasu bstan kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ched du bsgrub pa mi mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
18a3(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos bcu pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos so/ /kye rgyal
18a4(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyi mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ mtshan re re zhing bsod nams brgya ba'i
18a5(phal chen): mtshan yongs su dag par 'gyur ba 'di ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang po ste/ des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas
18a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung
18a7(phal chen): gnas phun sum tshogs pa'i spyod pa yongs su dag pa yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang /
18a8(phal chen): gdul ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyi mi non pa/ yongs su rdzogs pas
18b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /zhing yongs su dag par bya ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /
18b2(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang gzugs kyi sku blta ba don yod pa yongs su
18b3(phal chen): rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
18b4(phal chen): byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
18b5(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams gyi thabs mkhas
18b6(phal chen): pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing spros pa thams cad med par yang thugs su chud la/ dge ba'i sgo nas sangs rgyas
18b7(phal chen): kyi byin gyi brlabs kyang shin tu ston cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang po'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad
18b8(phal chen): la gzigs pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do/ /ma bcings ma grol ba dang gzung ba med cing bstsags pa med de/ yongs su rdzogs pa med par yang thugs su chud la sangs rgyas kyis chos
19a1(phal chen): thams cad la mnga' dam pa'ang brnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la mnga' bsgyur ba de yang / yang dag pa de kho na nyid ma nor ba rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad
19a2(phal chen): bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med la de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las rnam par mi 'da' yang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la yang / rab tu mkhyen pa 'di
19a3(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi/ sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan ma thams cad dang
19a4(phal chen): mi 'grogs shing / mtshan ma'i mngon par shes pa thams cad dang ma 'dres la de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa'i sgra'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud pas kyang gzugs kyi mtshan
19a5(phal chen): ma'i sku gzugs rnam par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan cing bshad pa'i ye shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba
19a6(phal chen): thams cad kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas/ mun pa med pa'i snang ba ston pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gsum pa'o/ /chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi mtha'
19a7(phal chen): yang ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba yang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa'am/ ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba yang ma yin pas de bzhin nyid kyis
19a8(phal chen): mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa brjod du med pas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba yang rab tu
19b1(phal chen): brjod cing kun tu gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bzhi pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
19b2(phal chen): rnams ni sku'i phrin las dang gsung gi phrin las dang / thugs kyi phrin las kyis mngon par 'du mdzad pa yang mi mnga' la/ yongs su blang ba mi mnga' bas bzhugs shing / rnam par phye ba med pa'i mthar
19b3(phal chen): thug pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la/ bgrang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul nges pa med pa'i mdzod du gyur cing / bgrang ba dang mngon par bsgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang /
19b4(phal chen): 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi tshul thugs su chud pa ye shes sgrib pa med pas gzigs pa rnams te/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems
19b5(phal chen): can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la/ rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par bsgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa lnga pa'o/ /chos thams cad
19b6(phal chen): lta ba med pas tha mi dad pa dang bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang mtshan nyid med pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med par rab tu mkhyen kyang /
19b7(phal chen): chos kyi rgyud shin tu nges pa yang dag par bsgrub cing / 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med pa yang dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa/ thams cad gzigs pa
19b8(phal chen): mkhyen par bya ba thams cad ma lus par gzigs par chos la mnga' bsgyur ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyams pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
20a1(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan mkhyen par bya ba chos de'i skyon med pa las rnam par ma
20a2(phal chen): 'das pa gnas med pa dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid kyi chos skyon med pas/ dus thams cad du gnas pa rab tu mkhyen te/ de la yang nyi ma gcig gam/ zla ba phyed dam/ lo gcig gam/
20a3(phal chen): lo brgya 'am/ bskal pa gcig pa dang / 'du bas rjes su bsnyag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang snga dro nas nyi ma phyed kyi dus dang /
20a4(phal chen): phyi dro nas snga dro'i dus dang / nyi ma gung nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma bgrangs pa'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phyed kyi dus dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang bskal pa gcig gi dus dang /
20a5(phal chen): tshad med grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med cing phyir mi ldog /rgyun chad par mi 'gyur/ bral bar
20a6(phal chen): mi 'gyur/ bar chad par mi 'gyur/ med par mi 'gyur/ 'jig par mi 'gyur g.yo bar mi 'gyur/ ring du mi 'gyur/ 'khor de na gnas pa nyid du yang rgyun chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs
20a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bdun pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rtag tu dus la bab par bzhugs pa ste/
20a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa grangs med pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o/ /
20b1(phal chen): so so yang dag par rig pa zad mi shes pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa thogs pa med pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa mtha' yas pa mnga' ba'o/ /thun mong ma yin pa'i
20b2(phal chen): so so yang dag par rig pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa de kho na dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o/ /so so yang dag par rig pa tshig
20b3(phal chen): gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa mnga' ba'o/ /chos thams cad so so yang dag par rig pa mnga' ba'o/ /bsam pa dang mos pa dang dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi tshul dang rnam grangs
20b4(phal chen): tshul ji ltar rnam par bkod pa bzhin dus 'tshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa rnams mdo sde dang de la thog ma dang dbus kyi tshul gyis yang
20b5(phal chen): dag par ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mying med kyang mying dang rigs su 'byung ba'i chos
20b6(phal chen): thams cad tshig dang yi ges shin tu sbyangs pa'i dbyangs mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/ mying 'das pa ma yin pa dang / mying ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / mying da ltar byung ba ma yin pa dang / mying sems can
20b7(phal chen): ma yin pa dang / mying zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma yin pa dang / mying yon tan ma yin pa dang / mying byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / mying sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / mying grangs ma yin pa dang / mying grangs
20b8(phal chen): med pa ma yin pa dang / mying skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / mying myed pa ma yin pa dang / mying yod pa ma yin pa dang / mying gcig pa ma yin pa dang / mying tha dad pa ma yin pa
21a1(phal chen): dang / mying thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang brda med pa dang / tshig gi lam med pa sgra dang bral ba dang / sgra'i rnam pa thams cad
21a2(phal chen): mi 'byung ba/ yongs su bsgrub pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa rnam pa gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pa mang po ma yin pa yang thugs su chud la/ brjod pa dang spyod pa thams cad la
21a3(phal chen): yang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes pa dag ste/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul mi mnga' ba dag go/ /mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la rab tu brtson pa dag go/ /rtog pa dang kun tu rtog pa yang yongs su
21a4(phal chen): rtog pa 'gags pa dag go/ /spyod pa thams cad la mi gnas par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dgu pa'o/ /sangs rgyas
21a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa tshor ba'i spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med pa dang / 'du byed kun tu rgyu ba med pa dang / rnam
21a6(phal chen): par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin gyis zhi ba rab tu mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye mched kyi rgyud med pa dang / khams rnams mi dmigs pa dang / chos thams cad mi
21a7(phal chen): 'jigs pa dang / chos thams cad bskyed du med cing / rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lta bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las med pa dang / rnam par smin pa med pa dang / spyod pas 'byung ba
21a8(phal chen): med pa dang / ma grub pa dang / ma byung ba dang / grangs kyis mi brjod pa dang yod pa ma yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang ma 'gags pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / skye ba med pa dang gnas
21b1(phal chen): pa med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa dang / rnam par btum ba med pa dang / sems can med pa dang / sems can med pa ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa
21b2(phal chen): ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin pa dang / rten med pa dang / rten med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thugs su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings thams cad shin tu bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam
21b3(phal chen): pa brnyes pa dag ste/ nges pa dang ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum rnam par dgod pa rnams la stobs bcus thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa bzhis rnam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi
21b4(phal chen): yul chen po dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra sgrog pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
21b5(phal chen): rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po gsum pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas
21b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin kyi brlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang /
21b7(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o/ /bcu gang zhe na/ phyogs bcu'i nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha'as gtugs
21b8(phal chen): pa'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du dga' ldan du skye ba bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mu med pa dag la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/
22a1(phal chen): kha dog tshad med pa gzi brjid tshad med pa snang ba tshad med pa/ dbyangs tshad med pa dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa tshad med pa gsung brjod pas rnam par dmyigs pa tshad med pa/ ting nge 'dzin tshad
22a2(phal chen): med pa la spyod pa/ shes rab dang ye shes kyi yul tshad med pa mnga' ba rnams lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ bdud dang bcas pa tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang
22a3(phal chen): bcas pa/ bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa/ lha dang mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ /byams pa chen po'i spyod yul thogs pa med pa dang /
22a4(phal chen): thabs thugs rje chen po'i sgo'i mthar thug pas sems can la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ /bsod nams kyi stobs dang / mnga' phun sum tshogs pa dang / dbang po rnam par sbyangs ba dang /
22a5(phal chen): cang shes kyi sems yongs su dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ /theg pa sna tshogs rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ /theg pa chen po
22a6(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do/ /'gro ba thams cad gnon pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
22a7(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las dang po'o/ /dga' ldan gyi pho brang nas 'phos pa med kyang yum gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i sku tha ma skye bar ston pa/ sgyu ma lta bur yongs
22a8(phal chen): su spyod pa/ sprul pa lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin kyi mthar thug pa/ mig yor lta bur rnam par dmigs pa/ nam mkha'i yul tshad med par khyab pa/ bzhed pa bzhin du skye ba yang chags pa mi mnga' ba
22b1(phal chen): smig sgyu lta bur bstan pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos la yang dag par gzhol ba/ gnas med pa'i ye shes la gnas pa/ rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral bas rnam par dag pa/ rgyan
22b2(phal chen): shin tu rgya che ba'i mdzod kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho brang chen po rin po che'i rgyan mang po dang ldan pa na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
22b3(phal chen): mdzad do/ /rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /yid la bya ba'i byin gyi brlabs chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /rnam par 'phrul pa'i mdzod chen po yang dag
22b4(phal chen): par bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /yum sku bskyed pa'i sku na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas
22b5(phal chen): kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po brnyes pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'jig rten byin gyis brlabs pa mtha' yas pas sangs
22b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /ting nge 'dzin chen po grangs myed pa la rnam par spyod cing / snyoms par 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag
22b7(phal chen): gis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /spyod pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bar du thogs ma dang dbus dang tha ma'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las
22b8(phal chen): mdzad do/ /sa 'di la gnyis su med pas thams cad mthar phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi grangs kyi skye ba yongs su ston te/ skye bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
23a1(phal chen): mdzad do/ /gzhon nur gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /byang chub sems dpar gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /
23a2(phal chen): mngon par 'byung bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas
23a3(phal chen): kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /thabs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs 'jig rten tshad med pa/ 'jig rten kun tu mtha' yas pa phyogs kyi
23a4(phal chen): dra ba'i rgyud dang / dus thams cad kyi 'jig rten ma lus pa thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /zhing gi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /las kyi rnam
23a5(phal chen): par smin pa ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /sems can gyi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /skye ba dang shi 'phos pa'i rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig
23a6(phal chen): rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /sprul pa chen po'i rgyud dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos dran pa'i sgo'i 'khor los kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
23a7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gnyis pa'o/ /dge bar spyod pa'i las rnam par dag cing gdung rabs thams cad du ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag pas/ sku tshe'i rgyud kyi tshul dang ldan pa sems
23a8(phal chen): can thams cad gdul ba thugs su chud pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad do/ /btsun mo'i 'khor kyi nang du bzhugs pa ston kyang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i
23b1(phal chen): tshul gyis gnas la bzhugs pa rnams sgra dang / tshig thams cad dang bral bar brtags pas/ dngos po thams cad dngos po med pa las byung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / dngos po thams cad
23b2(phal chen): shes pa la gzung bar bya ba dang / tshul khrims thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar thug par yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / snying rje chen pos 'gro ba mu med pa la rnam par blta bar bya ba dang / byams pa chen
23b3(phal chen): pos sems can med pa'i yul la rab tu rtogs par bya ba dang / dga' ba chen pos 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa khong du chud par bya ba dang / btang snyoms chen pos sems la dbang bsgyur ba la
23b4(phal chen): gnas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan gyis rang yongs su rgyas par byed par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus ma lus par mngon par bsgrub par bya ba dang / thams cad du gnas
23b5(phal chen): med pa'i lus yongs su rdzogs par byed par bya ba dang / 'khor thams cad rnam par dag par nan tan tu byed par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa rnam par rjod par rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / 'jig rten
23b6(phal chen): gyi dngos po la smod par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyes pa la rtog par bya ba mdzad cing spyod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par smin pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / ji ltar bkod pa'i
23b7(phal chen): tshul du sems can gdul ba dang / yongs su ma smin pa'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / yongs su smin pa rnams tshul bzhin du gdul ba dang / grangs med pa'i thabs mkhas
23b8(phal chen): pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog pa yongs su bstan pa dang / sgo sna tshogs nas chos kyi spyod pa rab tu brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kyi bsam pa
24a1(phal chen): sna tshogs par rnam par sbyang ba dang / thugs rje chen po las byung ba'i chos kyi sprin gyis mngon par sbyang ba dang / thams cad la skyob pa'i byams pa chen po bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum
24a2(phal chen): gyis yongs su brlan pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mngon pa dang / rnam par dmigs par btsun mo'i 'khor kyi nang du bstan pa yan chad du 'jig rten mtha' dang dbus med par sangs rgyas kyi
24a3(phal chen): phrin las yongs su bstan pa mdzad cing / ye shes kyi mthu chen po thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mngon par mkhyen pa sgrib pa med par bsgrub pa dang / chos rnam pa gsum gyi thabs
24a4(phal chen): mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i phrin las kyi mtha' dang / sku'i phrin las kyi mtha' shin tu rnam par dag pa dang / gsung gi phrin las ye shes nyams pa med pas rnam par dag pa dang / thugs kyi
24a5(phal chen): p hrin las kyi mtha' zab cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i thabs la mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don mdzad de 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
24a6(phal chen): gsum pa'o/ /rnam par rgyal ba chen po mnga' ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor rgyan rnam par phye ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong ba spangs te/ mngon par 'byung ba'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pas
24a7(phal chen): sems can rnams 'jig rten gyi gnas las bskyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten du gtogs pa thams cad mi rtag par shes par bya ba dang /
24a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi tshul la mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten gyi dga' ba la sred pa yongs su gcad pa dang / 'jig rten gyis nyon mongs pa byang zhing nub pa la yang dag par spyod
24b1(phal chen): par bya ba dang / sems can gyi don rjes su dran par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par 'byung ba'i don la rab tu gzhol ba dang / khyim pa'i tshul yongs su spang ba bstan pa dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos
24b2(phal chen): kyi sbyor ba la yang dag par gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongs su snang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor
24b3(phal chen): chen po brnyes pas sems can rnams kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu bstsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams kyi zhing bla na med par gyur par 'gro ba thams cad la bstan pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams
24b4(phal chen): cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus par 'gro ba thams cad la yang dag par brjod pa dang / bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don gzigs par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams rnam
24b5(phal chen): par dag pa'i sgor brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kha na ma tho ba med pa'i sgor bsgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ba'i sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi
24b6(phal chen): rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng bar mdzad cing mngon par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las bzhi pa'o/ /don gcig ma yin pa mkhyen pa dang ldan pa/
24b7(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rnams ni chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi
24b8(phal chen): dpung thams cad rab tu gzhom pa dang / sku'i byin gyi brlabs kyi mdzod kyis chos kyi dbyings kyi ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir byin gyi brlabs zad mi shes pa'i mthar thug pas mtha'
25a1(phal chen): rnam par spangs pa spyod pa tshad med pa rab tu brnyes pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul gyis rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi don dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan yang dag par bsgrub pa yongs su
25a2(phal chen): rdzogs pa 'jig rten gyis khams ma lus pa thams cad du gdan rnam par bkram pas yongs su rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpas rnam par dmigs pa/
25a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dam pa thob pa rnams kyi zhal du blta ba/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyad par can dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi
25a4(phal chen): dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis yang dag par bsam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo zab mo rab tu bskor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi yul tshad med pa brtsams pa/ byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i 'byung
25a5(phal chen): gnas su gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sna tshogs spyod pa la yang dag par gzhol ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa mnga' ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams
25a6(phal chen): thams cad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis byin du brlob pa'i yul mnga' ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis rnam par dmigs pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad tha mi dad pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i sa/
