25a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i mthu'i gnas la yon tan gyis khyad par thams cad rab tu brnyes nas bzhugs pa/ 'jig rten gyi rnam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar thug pa/ sems
25a8(phal chen): can gyi rnam pa thams cad dang / zhing gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa thams cad dang / yongs su smin par bya ba'i rnam pa thams
25b1(phal chen): cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / gdul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar thug pa rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad du
25b2(phal chen): mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'tshang rgya bas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las lnga pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
25b3(phal chen): kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar mdzad pa phyir mi ldog pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs
25b4(phal chen): pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen po'i tshul gyis thams cad ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos kyi mdzod mu med pa'i sgos snang bar byed pa'i tshul gyi chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor
25b5(phal chen): lo dang / ye shes nam mkha'i dbyings ltar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chags pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos thams cad kyi dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i tshul gyis sgrib pa med pa'i
25b6(phal chen): 'khor lo/ sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mig rnam par sbyong ba'i tshul gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi sgron ma'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs pa'i tshul gyis thams
25b7(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa'i chos brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur ba'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la stsogs pa
25b8(phal chen): rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa la/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ de ltar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang /
26a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las drug pa'o/ /sangs
26a2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni grong dang grong khyer dang grong rdal dang / rgyal po'i gnas su gshegs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ mi'i rgyal po'i gnas dang /
26a3(phal chen): lha'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / klu'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / dri za'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / nam mkha' lding gi rgyal
26a4(phal chen): po'i gnas dang / mi 'am ci'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang / srin po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / sha za'i rgyal po'i gnas dag tu gshegs pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan
26a5(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta ste/ grong khyer gyi sgor byon nas g.yo ba dang / 'od zer snang ba dang / long ba rnams mig 'thob pa dang / 'on pa rnams sgra thos par 'gyur ba dang /
26a6(phal chen): smyon pa rnams dran pa thob par 'gyur ba dang / gos med pa rnams gos thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams bde ba thob pa dang / rol mo'i cha byad ma dkrol ma brdungs par sgra yid du 'ong ba rang
26a7(phal chen): 'byin pa dang / rgyan snod na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas ma phog pa dang / ma bskyod ma dkrol bar bskyod cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dang / bya sna tshogs mang po'i sgra skad yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba dang /
26a8(phal chen): blta na gtang mi bra zhing mi 'thun pa med pa'i sku mthong bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po bstan
26b1(phal chen): pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ yongs su gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang /
26b2(phal chen): bskum pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /gshegs pa dang slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / 'chag pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / gzims pas kyang
26b3(phal chen): sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /chos bstan pa dang / mi gsung bar bzhugs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul dang /
26b4(phal chen): yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul sems can bsam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho dang
26b5(phal chen): ldan pa 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad rgyu zhing 'byung ba dang ldan pa dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos shin tu brtan pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang ldan pa/ sngon 'grogs 'grogs pa'i byang chub sems
26b6(phal chen): dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku gzugs blta na mi ngoms pa'o zhes bya bar gzhol ba dang /
26b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas rnams skye bar dkon no zhes bya bar yid ches par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos pa ni bsod nams kyi chos dkar po'i 'byung
26b8(phal chen): gnas su gyur pa'o/ /zhes sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa yid la byed pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa skye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang /
27a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bsngags pa ni mtha' yas pa'o zhes bya bar yang dag par lta ba dang / ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par bsgrub pa dang /
27a2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba dang mos pa'i tshul thams cad kyis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mnyes par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni yon tan mtha' yas pa'o zhes khong du chud par
27a3(phal chen): byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can thams cad la mngon tu gyur par rtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can gyi ris bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas su gyur par sems pa dang /
27a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa ni zhing thams cad na snang bar khong du chud pa dang / de lta bu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'byung bas 'jig rten thams cad na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can
27a5(phal chen): rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /dad par bya ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / thal mo sbyar bar byas pa dang / rjes su ston pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du
27a6(phal chen): mthong ba dang 'dzum pa bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dga' ba'i sems kyis mos par byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo nas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi
27a7(phal chen): phrin las mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas rjes su dran par gyur pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas mthong bar
27a8(phal chen): 'dod par byas pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku kha dog dang dbyibs kyi rnam pa tshad med pa bstan
27b1(phal chen): pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos par bya bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan
27b2(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ de dag la stsogs pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad pa rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya
27b3(phal chen): stong brjod du med pa dag / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / mthu dang 'dul ba ji lta ba'i tshul las mi 'da' bar 'byung ngo / /
27b4(phal chen): de ltar sangs rgyas kyi phrin las 'jig rten thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa dang bsam pa la gnas/ dge ba rgya che ba tshad med pa dag phyir mi ldog pa'i yul dang / snying rje
27b5(phal chen): chen pos rab tu bskul ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam gyis yongs su skyo ba med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mkhyen pa'i stobs dang / shugs kyis 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ste/
27b6(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bdun pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dgon pa la bzhugs sam/ zhi bar bzhugs sam/
27b7(phal chen): dben par bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs sam/ ting nge 'dzin chen po'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ gcig pu dgyes par bzhugs sam/ sku myi snang
27b8(phal chen): bar bzhugs sam/ ye shes zab mo'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi stobs tshad med pa la bzhugs sam/ sku yongs su spyod pa mi mthong bar bzhugs kyang rung
28a1(phal chen): ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gzhan gyis mi tshugs pa'i ye shes dang / smon lam gyi tshul gyis mos pa bzhin du 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la
28a2(phal chen): rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ste/ sangs rgyas lha yongs su tshol bas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /sangs rgyas klu yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun
28a3(phal chen): mi 'chad do/ /sangs rgyas gnod sbyin yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas mi'am ci yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas lto 'phye chen po yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas srin po yongs su
28a4(phal chen): tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas mi dang mi ma yin pa yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas nyan thos dang / sangs rgyas rang sangs rgyas dang / sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs
28a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /chos ston pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /sangs rgyas gcig brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /sangs rgyas
28a6(phal chen): thams cad brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad gcig tu brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /
28a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gcig rnam par phye ste/ spyod pa tha dad pa brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /'jig rten gyi yul sangs rgyas kyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas
28a8(phal chen): kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /sangs rgyas kyi yul 'jig rten gyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /yul ma yin pa sangs rgyas kyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas
28b1(phal chen): kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do/ /nyin mtshan dang zla ba yar kham mar kham dang / zla ba dang / lo bsgrang bar bzhugs pa dang / yongs su bzhugs pa nas/ de bzhin du bskal pa brjod du med pa yang
28b2(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i bar du bzhugs pa dang / yongs su bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mi 'chad do/ /'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
28b3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las brgyad pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la 'byung gnas lta bu/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa kun la rnam par spyod pa
28b4(phal chen): lta bu/ sangs rgyas rnams la dad pa lta bu/ sems khong du chud par bya ba la shin tu mos pa lta bu/ dbang po rnams la bsgrub pa lta bu/ sems can skye dgu thams cad la 'dul ba lta bu/
28b5(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad la mos pa lta bu/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la 'byung ba lta bu/ byang chub tu zhugs pa rnams la bskul ba lta bu/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa rnams la ye shes kyi
28b6(phal chen): snang ba lta bu dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten mi rtag par ston pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par brjod pa dang / phrin las mdzad pa'i mthar
28b7(phal chen): thug par bstan pa dang / chos kyi rgyud tu nyams pa med pa'i dngos por brjod pa dang / srid pa'i tshul rtsa ba nas chad par rjod pa dang / sems can thams cad skyo bar bya bar bstan pa dang /
28b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rjes su 'gro ba'i sems su mthun par bya ba dang / sku tshe'i mtha' lta bur sems can rnams kyis shes par bya ba dang / sems can rnams kyis 'jig rten thams cad du dga' bar
29a1(phal chen): bya ba med par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams la ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gcig nas/ gcig tu brgyud pa mnyes par gyis shig par bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom
29a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba bstan du mi rung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'jig rten rnams kyi rtsol ba bskyed pa dang sangs rgyas la dmigs par brtson pa'i sems la dgod pa dang /
29a3(phal chen): yun tu dran pa rnam par dag pas de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba'i rnam par rtog pa bskyed pa dang / skye ba'i dbang po phyir bzlog cing yongs su dag par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas la mos pa bskyed
29a4(phal chen): pa dang / skyo bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i rkyen 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyin par dgongs pa mdzad pa dang /
29a5(phal chen): sku thams cad bshig ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung gis sems can rnams yongs su gzung ba mdzad pa dang / 'jig rten rnam par 'khrug pa dang / dregs shing myos pa'i sems can
29a6(phal chen): rnams sdom pa la bkod pa mdzad cing / yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
29a7(phal chen): phrin las dgu pa'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/ 'jig rten thams cad na sems can rnams smre sngags 'don cing ngu ba dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / 'chi ma 'byin pa dang /
29a8(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas zhe'am/ thugs rje chen po zhe 'am/ ded dpon chen po zhe 'am/ phan par bzhed pa thugs brtse ba can zhe 'am/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten
29b1(phal chen): gyi sems can thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur pa/ mgon du gyur pa/ rten du gyur pa/ bla na med pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing nub par gyur to zhes 'am/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'byung bar
29b2(phal chen): dka'o/ /zhes rnam pa de lta bur smre sngags 'don cing / mya ngan byed pa dang / sangs rgyas mthong ba rjes su dran pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / yid la bya ba de dang de dag gi sgor sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad
29b3(phal chen): med pa rgyun mi 'chad do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshe/ 'di lta ste sems can rnams kyi sems dad par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams dad pas
29b4(phal chen): mchod par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par spyod par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongs su smin par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongs su sbyang bar bya
29b5(phal chen): ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams gdul ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams kyi bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod
29b6(phal chen): pas dmigs par bya ba'i dbang dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten rnam pa sna tshogs su brgyan pas/ phyogs dang yul sna tshogs su sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bstsags par bya ba'i
29b7(phal chen): dbang gis sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang / ring bsrel byin kyis rlob ste/ lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang /
29b8(phal chen): mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi'i gnas thams cad du 'dul ba dang / mos pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du/ sku gdung dang ring bsrel byin gyis brlob po/ /rang gi sku rnam
30a1(phal chen): par phye ste/ sku gdung dang ring srel tshad med pa grangs med pa dpag tu med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa byin gyis brlabs/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten gyi sangs rgyas
30a2(phal chen): kyi sku gdung 'jig rten thams cad du rnam par phye ba'i de'i yul dang / phyogs kyi klu'i gnas dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang /
30a3(phal chen): mi'i gnas dang / srin po'i gnas dag tu sku gdung dang / ring bsrel mchod pa byed par 'gyur bas/ sku gdung gi ring srel dang dbu dang / phyag sen gyi mchod rten dang / sangs rgyas bzhugs pa'i mchod rten
30a4(phal chen): la 'gro ba thams cad nges par sangs rgyas dran par 'gyur te/ chos la rab tu rten par 'gyur ro/ /dge 'dun la dad pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /yul dang phyogs kyi gnas de dang de dag tu yang rgyun
30a5(phal chen): mi 'chad par sangs rgyas mchod pa la brtson pa'i bsam pas sbyin pa yongs su gtong bar 'gyur ro/ /bsod nams byed par 'gyur ro/ /mtho ris de dang de yongs su dag pa rab tu 'thob par
30a6(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /rigs dang rgyud kyi bdag nyid che ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /longs spyod chen po dang / 'khor rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa nyams su
30a7(phal chen): myong bar 'gyur ro/ /log par ltung ba med pa'i lam yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas byung ba don yod pa rab tu bsgrub par 'gyur ro/ /chos dkar po la gnas pa yongs su rdzogs par byed par
30a8(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /khams gsum pa las 'byung ba'i lam yongs su sbyong bar 'gyur ro/ /theg pa gang la dad pa'i smon lam gyis nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag de dag la drin du gzo ba rab tu 'thob par
30b1(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la rten pa dang / skyabs btsol ba dang / mgon btsal ba dang / dpung nyen btsal ba'i sems bskyed par 'gyur te/ de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
30b2(phal chen): yongs su mya ngan las 'das kyang yon bsam gyis mi khyab par sbyong ba/ bsod nams zad mi shes pa'i yon tan gyi gnas dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten du byung na de ltar
30b3(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam pa mang po rab tu bstsags pas bsod nams kyi tshogs rab tu rdzogs par 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las bcu pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i
30b4(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so/ /de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin brlabs ma gtogs par
30b5(phal chen): lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis tshad gzung bar mi nus pa'o/ /'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'jug par mi nus pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i
30b6(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po rnam pa gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas bcom
30b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni lung bstan pa thams cad ston pa la gnyis su med par spyod do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa la brtson pa'i rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa brjod
30b8(phal chen): du med pa 'byam klas pa rnams la gnyis su med par spyod do/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi don ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pas gnyis su med pa'i sku rnam par mdzad do/ /'das pa dang /
31a1(phal chen): ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rang bzhin gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ /'byung ba dang byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang /
31a2(phal chen): da ltar byung ba gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gnyis su med pas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gcig par rab tu mkhyen cing ston pa thugs su chud pa
31a3(phal chen): mnga' ba'o/ /sangs rgyas gcig dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa dang / 'dul ba mdzad pa'i rnam par dmigasu med
31a4(phal chen): par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ /'jig rten gyi chos thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ /'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i
31a5(phal chen): rtsa ba thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig ste/ gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po gnyis su med pa'i
31a6(phal chen): chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa'i chos thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa rnams so/ /bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom
31a7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i ye shes thugs su chud pa la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs rje chen po mi nyams pa la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
31a8(phal chen): ni smon lam ji lta ba bzhin du 'byung ba la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su mi gtong ba la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po med pa la
31b1(phal chen): gnas pa'i chos nyid la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku skal ba mnyam pa tha mi dad cing don yod pa la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu mnyam par gzhag
31b2(phal chen): pa'i thugs la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad nyams pa med par gzhol ba la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i dgongs pas rnam par spyod pa
31b3(phal chen): la bzhugs pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha'i mtshan nyid la bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
31b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos thams cad la bzhugs pa rnams so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad
31b5(phal chen): ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'das pa bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / ma 'ongs pa
31b6(phal chen): bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / da ltar byung ba bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / tshig gi lam mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi
31b7(phal chen): rgyud mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / sems can kyi bsam pa dang shes pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen po dang / rnam pa sna tshogs
31b8(phal chen): su rnam par gnas pa'i mtshan nyid kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la bsam pa tshad med pa yongs su mi gtong bas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'bar bar bya ba dang / yongs su rdzogs par bya ba mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /
32a1(phal chen): chos thams cad 'tshang rgya ba'i mkhyen pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud thams cad rnam par dbye ba'i ye shes gzigs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /
32a2(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi myig 'phrul gyi rnam pa lta bur dbye ba thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa'o// //
32a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bzhi pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs chen po/ /stobs dam pa stobs tshad myed pa stobs bdag nyid che ba stobs thug myed pa/ stobs
32a4(phal chen): mi mnyam pa stobs snying po dang ldan pa/ stobs myi shigs pa/ stobs 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis myi khyab pa/ stobs sems can thams cad kyis myi 'phrog pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyal mtshan stobs po che/
32a5(phal chen): dpa' bo chen po'i stobs rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ni pha rol gyi gnod pa thams cad kyis myi shigs myi chod pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi yul thams cad kyis sku tshe'i dbang po nyams par myi
32a6(phal chen): nus pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi bskal pa'i mye'i gdung bas 'tshig par myi nus pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'jig par gtogs pa'i chu'i phung por 'grongs par myi 'gyur ba'o/ /bdud
32a7(phal chen): thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad dang / lha thams cad kyi dpung dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang / myi'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang mi dang / myi ma yin pa thams cad kyi dpung dang /
32a8(phal chen): sha za dang / srin po thams cad kyi dpung dang / sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi dpung gis brgol bar dka' ba'o/ /rdo rje ri rab gyi ri tsam gyi char pa dang / khor yug gi ri chen po tsam 'am/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i tsam
32b1(phal chen): gyi rdo rje'i char bab kyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ba spu gcig kyang 'gul bar myi 'gyur/ g.yo bar myi 'gyur te/ bag tsha ba'i shes
32b2(phal chen): mi mnga'o/ /bzhugs sam bzhengs sam bzhud dam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ spyod lam 'gyur ba myed do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gang na bzhugs pa'i yul de dang de'i 'khor dag tu yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes na kun tu
32b3(phal chen): 'bab par myi 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas kyi zham ring ba rnams la yang gnod par myi 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas kyi byin kyis brlabs pa'i sems can rnams la yang gnod par myi 'gyur zhing / mi g.yo na de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku lta
32b4(phal chen): smos kyang ci dgos te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dang po'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dgyes na/
32b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ri rab kyi ri dang bcas pa/ khor yug dang khor yug chen po'i ri dang bcas pa/ rgya mtsho dang / ri dang nags tshal thibs po dang / sems can
32b6(phal chen): gnas pa'i gnas tha dad pa kun dang / bcas pa de lta bu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig tu btsud de/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par bzhag kyang / de bzhin gshegs
32b7(phal chen): pa'i byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par sems can rnams kyis shes par myi nus so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ni de snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams sku'i ba spu'i khung bu gcig gis bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha' bskal pa'i mur
32b8(phal chen): thug par bsnams shing / gshegs sam/ bzhugs sam/ bzhengs sam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs skad cig tsam yang skyo ba mi mnga'o/ /chad cing dub par myi 'gyur ro/ /mthu dang
33a1(phal chen): stobs la yongs su nyam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o/ /spyod lam rnam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ nam mkha' ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams
33a2(phal chen): cad 'dzin kyang skyo ba med do/ /dub pa med do/ /gnod pa med do/ /med par mi 'gyur ro/ /mi g.yo mi 'byung mi 'jig go/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang ba spu'i khung bu gcig du 'jig rten gyi khams
33a3(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad bsnams kyang / de'i rgyus thugs skad cig tsam du yang mi bde ba'i sku nyams mi 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i
33a4(phal chen): rgyal mtshan gyi chos gnyis pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams gshegs stabs gcig tu bzhug pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi khams
33a5(phal chen): yongs su 'da' zhing / dgongs pa bskyed pa gcig gis bskal pa tha dad pa'i rim par sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba bsnyed 'byung ba mdzad do/ /de lta bur gshigs pas
33a6(phal chen): bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du gshegs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud ji snyed pa'i bskal par bzhud de/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
33a7(phal chen): kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi/ 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du khor kun tu rgya che zhing yangs pa'i 'khor yug chen po'i rdo rje'i ri dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rnam pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la bsres pa snyed kyi rdul
33a8(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed kyang / de la bsres pa de snyed ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu ji lta ba bzhin du/ sku'i ba spu'i khung bu thams cad du btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu yang sems can thams cad de snyed du gyur
33b1(phal chen): la/ de dag thams cad bsnams te/ de snyed kyi ba spu'i khung bu tshul de bzhin du bshams te/ thugs bskyed pa de lta bus/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ phyogs kyi dra ba
33b2(phal chen): thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud 'grangs pa sngon gyi mthar gtogs pa nas bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug
33b3(phal chen): par/ de bzhin gshegs pas bskal pa thams cad zad par gyur kyang de bzhin gshegs pa bzhud pa la brtson pa ni nyams par mi 'gyur ro/ /sku nyams chung bar mi 'gyur ro/ /dgongs pa rnam par 'khrug par mi 'gyur
33b4(phal chen): ro/ /ting nge 'dzin nyams par mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan
33b5(phal chen): gyi chos gsum pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni bsod snyoms gcig bzhes nas bskal pa brjod du med par skyil mo krung gcig bcas pas/ nyin mtshan gyi rgyud tu sngon gyi mtha' dang /
33b6(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtha'i mur gtogs pa'i bskal pa bzhugs kyang / sku mi g.yo zhing bde ba'i dam pa la spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab par rnam par spyod kyang / sems can 'ga' tsam la yang sangs rgyas
33b7(phal chen): kyi phrin las rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yongs su bkod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gcig gi lus kyang 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas
33b8(phal chen): kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed tsam du che ba de lta bur gyur la/ sems can gcig gi lus kyi tshad ji tsam pa de tsam gyi lus su sems can thams cad gyur la/ sems can de dag re re'i gzugs kyang
34a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi lcid ji tsam yod pa de tsam du gyur te/ sems can gcig gi lci ba bzhin du sems can thams cad re re'i lcid kyang de tsam du gyur te/ sems can de dag thams cad de
34a2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag sor gyi rtse mo gcig la/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par bsnams te/ phyag sor gyi rtse mo gcig gis ji ltar bsnams pa de bzhin du phyag sor thams cad kyi rtse mo la 'ang / de tsam
34a3(phal chen): re re bsnams kyang / de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa la sku mnyel ba 'am/ dgongs pa dub par mi 'gyur te/ thugs bskyed pa'i cha shas shin tu phra ba gcig tsam du yang sdug bsngal myi bde ba skye bar myi 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin
34a4(phal chen): du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rnam pa la 'jug pa re re dang de lta bu la 'jug pa nam mkha'i khams ma lus pa'i dbyings kyis klas pa/ chos kyi
34a5(phal chen): dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa skra'i rtse mo'i gzhal ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa thams cad re re zhing yang / skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal te/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyis kun tu khyab pa thams cad
34a6(phal chen): ma lus pa'i skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyi tshad kyis nam mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa thams cad du zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam 'di'i tshul dang / skyil mo krung gcig tu bzhugs pa'i spyod pas/ sngon
34a7(phal chen): gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad par mdzad de/ bskal pa 'da' bar mdzad cing / bskal pa la rab tu 'jug ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i
34a8(phal chen): stobs sangs rgyas gyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig la/ dbu sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu
34b1(phal chen): phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs te/ dbu re re yang ljags sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs nas/ de dag re res kyang dbyangs kyi yan lag dang sgra skad
34b2(phal chen): kyi gsung / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed re re brjod de/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad cing dbyangs kyi yan lag dang sgra skad
34b3(phal chen): kyi gsung re res kyang mdo sde sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bshad la mdo sde re re la 'ang chos bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab
34b4(phal chen): tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa gcig las kyang chos kyi tshig dang yi ge sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed brjod par gyur la/ chos bstan pa gcig las
34b5(phal chen): ji lta ba de bzhin du chos bstan pa thams cad las kyang de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang yi ge brjod de/ de ltar brjod pas bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan pa/ bskal pa sangs
34b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad par gyur kyang / da dung gzhan yang bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du brgyud cing rab tu ston pa'i tshul gyis
34b7(phal chen): rnam grangs 'dis bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la/ rnam grangs 'di 'dra bas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad la sems can
34b8(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa snyed kyi bskal pa 'das par gyur te/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad cing 'das par byas kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa chos thams cad snang ba'i 'khor lo bskor
35a1(phal chen): ba dang / chos thams cad rab tu shes par bstan cing lung bstan pa dang / the rtsom thams cad rab tu gcod pa'i 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar byed pa'i/ chos kyi 'khor lo
35a2(phal chen): bskor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad brjod pa'i rgyun dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo
35a3(phal chen): bskor ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad ma lus par ye shes kyi sgron ma chen pos rgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / so so yang dag par rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo
35a4(phal chen): bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad de/ sangs rgyas kyi sku gcig gi byin gyis brlabs kyi ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi 'khor lo'i sprin chen po dpe thams cad dang / dpe med par rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du chos kyi
35a5(phal chen): dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal ba ma lus pa thams cad chags pa med par rnam par dbye bas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i
35a6(phal chen): yang brjod du med pa snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa de snyed de snyed du dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal par sprul pa mdzad cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku thams cad las de
35a7(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi dbu mnga' bar 'gyur la gzhung de bzhin du dbu re re la yang de snyed de snyed kyi ljag mnga' bar gyur te/ ljag re re las kyang de snyed de snyed kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag
35a8(phal chen): dang / sgra skad kyi gsungs chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad par byung la/ dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsungs de dag re res kyang de
35b1(phal chen): snyed de snyed kyi mdo sde bshed par gyur la mdo sde de dag re re la yang de snyed de snyed kyi/ chos bstan pa la rab tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa de dag de re re las kyang / de snyed de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang yi ger brjod par gyur la/ chos
35b2(phal chen): kyi tshig dang yi ge de dag re res kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad dbyangs kyi rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad go bar mdzad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs la dub pa myi mnga' ste/
35b3(phal chen): nyams par mi 'gyur la thogs pa myi mnga' zhing dma' bar myi 'gyur ro/ /de lta bu'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor yang bskal pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bar du rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
35b4(phal chen): mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan chos lnga pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs dpal gyi be'us brgyan pa/ rdo rje chen po ltar shin tu bstan par grub pa
35b5(phal chen): mnga' ba dag ste/ de dag byang chub kyi shing drung du byon na bdud sdig to can gyis sems can thams cad snyed kyi bdud kyi sde/ gzugs sna tshogs can shin tu mi sdug pa/ 'jigs 'jigs ltar 'dug pa/ rab tu sdang ba'i
35b6(phal chen): gzugs can 'jig rten thams cad shin tu 'jigs pa'i gzugs can rab tu skyi g.ya' ba bskyed pa'i gzugs can/ bdud shin tu mi sdug pa'i gzugs 'tshang bar btsog por 'jigs pa/ 'jigs pa chen po bskyed pa/
35b7(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad gsod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad phung bar byed pa de lta bu sha stag gis/ byang chub kyi shing drung dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / nam mkha'i dbyings
35b8(phal chen): kyi mthar thug par gang bar gzigs kyang byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la bsnyings pa myi mnga'o/ /bag tsha ba mi mnga' 'o/ /
36a1(phal chen): ba spu gcig kyang g.yo ba myed do/ /dgongs pa'i cha shas shin tu phra ba 'ga' tsam gyis kyang de ltar rnam pa tha dad pa'i gzugs la mtshan ma rnam pa tha dad pa 'dzin pa myi mnga' ste/ shin tu bstan no/ /g.yo ba myed do/ /mi
36a2(phal chen): sgul to/ /'gyur ba myed do/ /rnam par rtog pa med do/ /shin tu zhi'o/ /snyengs pa dang bag tsha ba thams cad dang shin tu bral lo/ /sdug pa dang khong khro ba shin tu spongs so/ /sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa rgyun mi 'chad de/ byams pa chen po'i
36a3(phal chen): stobs dang ldan pa'o/ /thugs rje chen po'i gnas kyi dbang po'i shin tu dben pa'o/ /bag tsha ba mi mnga' ba'i dgongs pa dang ldan pa'o/ /dgongs pa shin tu bstan zhing nyams pa mi mnga' ba'o/ /tshur zil gyi mi non la
36a4(phal chen): phar zil gyi gnon pa'i dgongs pa dang ldan pa ste/ bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad shin tu zil kyis gnon to/ /shin tu spa bskong ngo / /de ltar
36a5(phal chen): zil gyi mnan te/ spa bskong pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la skyabs tshol lo/ /de dag la'ang bcom ldan 'das de dag cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdul ba mdzad pa nye bar
36a6(phal chen): bsgrub ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir myi ldog par 'gyur ro/ /'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan
36a7(phal chen): gyi chos drug pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung thogs pa med pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa de dang / de dag thams cad du sems can rnams 'dul ba'i don gyi rnam
36a8(phal chen): par dmyigs par kun tu khyab pa 'byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsungs de ni ri rnams la thogs pa myed do/ /ri rab la thogs pa myed do/ /rin po che'i ri la thogs pa myed do/ /'khor yug dang 'khor yug
36b1(phal chen): chen po la thogs pa med do/ /lha'i khyim la thogs pa med do/ /klu'i khyim la thogs pa myed do/ /gnod sbyin gyi khyim la thogs pa med do/ /dri za'i khyim la thogs pa med do/ /lha ma yin gyi khyim la thogs pa med do/ /
36b2(phal chen): nam mkha' lding gi khyim la thogs pa med do/ /myi'am ci'i khyim la thogs pa med do/ /lto 'phye chen po'i khyim la thogs pa med do/ /mi dang mi ma yin pa'i khyim la thogs pa med do/ /gal te brgya la 'jig
36b3(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad na yod pa'i sgra chen po 'jig rten rnams tha dad pa'i sgras/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gang ste/ ca co 'dres par gyur kyang / de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i gsung
36b4(phal chen): ni 'dul ba'i sems can rnams kyi rna ba'i rnam par dmigs pa la sgrib pa med pa yin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsungs 'ba' shig de dag gi rnam par dmigs pa la/ lhang nge lham me lhan ne ste go
36b5(phal chen): bar mdzad pa'i tshig dang / yi ge rnams kyang rlag par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bdun pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs
36b6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs ni chags pa mi mnga' ba ste/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par yongasu sbyang pa'o/ /'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs
36b7(phal chen): rgyas thams cad dang / rgyan gcig tu gyur pa'o/ /rnyog pa med cing rnam par dang ste shin tu gsal ba'o/ /bdag gi zhes bya ba mi mnga' ba'o/ /chos thams cad la mi gnas pa'o/ /nang na gnas pa ma yin pa'o/ /phyi
36b8(phal chen): rol na gnas pa ma yin pa'o/ /ma skyes pa'o/ /dmigs pa thams cad kyis dben pa'o/ /zhi zhes gnas myed pa'o/ /rtsom pa med pa'o/ /'du shes sna tshogs thams cad la mi gnas pa'o/ /dngos po'i
37a1(phal chen): rnam par rtog pa thams cad 'gags pa'o/ /rang bzhin gyi 'od dang zhing gsal ba'o/ /yongasu dag pa'o/ /dmigs pa dang yid la byas pa thams cad dang ma 'dres pa'o/ /chos thams cad nyon mongs
37a2(phal chen): pa med pa'i yul dang ldan pa'o/ /yang dag pa'i mtha' 'dod chags dang bral bas dag pa'o/ /chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa'i mthar thugs pa'o/ /chos kyi dbyings kun nas mi zad pa dang ldan pa'o/ /'du shes kyi
37a3(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad kyi tshad dang tshad med pa dang bral ba'o/ /'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi brjod pa thams cad 'gags pa'o/ /tshigs gi lam gyis brjod du med pa'i mthar thugs pa'i yul lo/ /mi zad pa dang chags
37a4(phal chen): pa med pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'o/ /ye shes sngon du 'gro ba'o/ /stobs bcu'i rgyan du gyur pa'o/ /chos thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'o/ /thabs mkhas pa 'byung ba'o/ /chos sna tshogs dang chos du ma dang /
37a5(phal chen): chos thams cad shin tu bstan pa dang mi 'gal ba'o/ /dus gsum tha dad pa med pa'o/ /chos kyi dbyings thams cad du chos gzhi med pa thams cad kyi mnga' ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pa'o/ /chos thams cad la
37a6(phal chen): mnga' ba'i 'byung gnas dang / mdzod du gyur pa'o/ /chos kyi tshul thams cad dgongs pa khyad par du rmongs pa med pa'o/ /zhing gi rgyud du gtogs pa thams cad dang phyogs kyi dra ba dang / rgyud 'byam klas pa ma lus pa
37a7(phal chen): thams cad la mi gnas pa bstan zhing mi g.yo la nyams pa med pa'i ye shes kyis rab tu gzigs pa/ chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa zag pa thams cad yongs su zad pa dgongs pa rnam par grol zhing
37a8(phal chen): zag pa mi mnga' ba dang / shes rab rnam par grol bas shin tu rnam par grol ba yang dag pa'i mtha' myi zad pas klas pa/ chags pa med par rnam par spyod pa rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa dus gsum thams cad du sgrib
37b1(phal chen): pa med par 'byung ba/ sems can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad ma lus par thugs skad cig gis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs
37b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos brgyad pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni sku mi mnga' ba ste/ rang bzhin gcig tu gyur la sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul tshad med
37b3(phal chen): pa'i sku'o/ /mtha' dang dbus med par yongs su grub pa'i sku'o/ /'jig rten thams cad kyi zad par mi nus pa'i sku'o/ /khams gsum pas gos pa med pa'i sku'o/ /rten pa'i skus rnam par dmigs pa'o/ /lhag pa'i
37b4(phal chen): bsam pa dang rjes su dran pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi sku'i rang bzhin yang dag par bstan pa'o/ /bden pa med pa'o/ brdzun pa med pa'i sku mnyam pa nyid kyis yongs su dag pa'o/ /chos kyi sku bzhud pa dang byon pa med pa'i
37b5(phal chen): sku'o/ /'dus ma byas pas 'jig pa med pa'i sku'o/ /mtshan nyid med pas mtshan nyid gcig pa'i chos kyi sku'i rang bzhin no/ /yul na mi gnas pa dang phyogs na mi gnas pa'i sku'o/ /ma lus pa thams cad kyi
37b6(phal chen): lus kyi sku'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gis mthu phyung ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no/ /lus thams cad du yongs su gzhol ba'i sku sna tshogs su rnam par dmigs pa mdzad kyang
37b7(phal chen): chos kyi sku'i tshul gyi rjes su 'brang ba'o/ /ye shes kun tu snang ba'i snying po can no/ /sku yongs kyi mdzod du gyur pa'o/ /chos kyi dbyings rnam pa tha dad pa med pa shin tu bstan pa'i sku'o/ /khams ma lus pa thams
37b8(phal chen): cad rgyas par 'gengs pas/ kun tu khyab pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no/ /mi g.yo mi dgongs pa'i sku rnam par dag pa'o/ /yod pa ma yin med pa'ang ma yin pa'i tshul dang tshul ma yin par rab tu brjod pa'i sku'o/ /sems can gyi mos pa
38a1(phal chen): rnam pa sna tshogs 'dus par gyur pa'i sku'o/ /'gags pa'ang ma yin ma 'gags pa'ang ma yin pas 'dul ba ston pa'i sku'o/ /yon tan rin po che thams cad yang dag par ston pa'i sku'o/ yon tan rin po che
38a2(phal chen): thams cad yang dag par 'byung bas shin tu 'phags pa'i sku'o/ /chos thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi de bzhin nyid du yang dag par sgrub pa'i sku'o/ /rang bzhin gyis rab tu zhi zhing sgrib pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i sku'o/ /thogs
38a3(phal chen): pa mi mnga' bas chos thams cad thugs su chud pa'i sku'o/ /thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyis rnam par dag cing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du shin tu rnam par phye ba'i sku'o/ /phyir mi ldog cing sgrib pa mi mnga'
38a4(phal chen): la/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pas ye shes thams cad rjes su 'brang zhing / yang dag par gzhol bas thugs su chud pa'i sku te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu' bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal
38a5(phal chen): mtshan gyi chos dgu pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes mnyam pa med pa dang / mnyam pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs su chud pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams
38a6(phal chen): cad kyi byung ba'o/ /mngon par sgrub pa'i spyod pa khyad par du 'phags pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis yongs su rdzogs par byas so/ /
38a7(phal chen): tha dad pa med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis byung ba'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho'i spyod pa'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud pa'o/ /smon lam dang spyod pa chen po
38a8(phal chen): yongs su mi 'dogs pa'o/ /spyod pa thams cad mi mnyam pa med pas yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o/ /spyod pa'i stobs la theg par dka' ba'i spyod pa thams cad kyis mngon par byung ba'o/ /spyod pa thams cad kyis
38b1(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa legs par spyad pas rgyud dma' ba med pa'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyis tshad med par spyod pa'o/ /ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi spyod yul mtha' yas pa'o/ /
38b2(phal chen): lam thams cad kyi rab tu brjod pa ma yin pa'o/ /lam gyi yul med pa'o/ /lam thams cad la rab tu bzhugs pa'o/ /ye shes dam pa'i stobs kyi tshul mkhyen pa'o/ /bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas chos kyi char 'bebs pa'i 'khor
38b3(phal chen): lo dang ldan pa'o/ /dge ba dris pa dang ma dris pa la rjes su 'thun pa'i chos kyi tshul ston pa mkhyen pa'o/ /mnyam pa med pa dang mnyam pas shin tu dag pa'o/ /sku dang thugs dang gsungs gi yang dag par spyod pa rnams la phrin las gsum
38b4(phal chen): yongs su dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bsgoms pas brnyeso/ /sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pas brnyes pa'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs thams cad bskyod pa'i don du sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi mdzad pa thams cad rab tu 'byung ba'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i
38b5(phal chen): gnas kyi bstan pa tshad med pa'i gnas rtsa ba med pa dang ldan pa'o/ /mngon par shes pa'i ye shes thams cad kyi mthar thug par mi 'gyur ba'o/ /'jig rten gyi sems kyi spyod pa'i shes pa thams cad kyis
38b6(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o/ /chos thams cad ma lus par mkhyen cing gzigs pas sems can thams cad yongs su skyob pa'o/ /dus gsum yangs pa thams cad kyi tshul shin tu phra ba mtha' dang dbus med pa ma
38b7(phal chen): lus par mkhyen pa'o/ /'jig rten las 'das pa'i don mkhyen pa'i phyir phra ba'i ye shes thugs su chud pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rnam par dag pa phyir mi ldog pa'i ye shes kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
38b8(phal chen): brjod du med pa 'jig rten thams cad du sbyor ba'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi sku grangs pa thams cad thugs su chud pa'i ye shes kyis yi ge med pa'i chos thugs su chud pa'o/ /yi ge sna tshogs rnam par
39a1(phal chen): phye ba dang / yi ge thams cad smos shing brjod pa mkhyen pas/ brjod du med pa thugs su chud pa'o/ /kun tu bzang po'i ye shes kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i chos spyad pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'o/ /dam
39a2(phal chen): bcas pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can thams cad kyi lus dang skye mched ji ltar dgongs pa'i skad cig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyi chos thams cad khong du chud par ston pa mkhyen pa'o/ /chos thams cad kyi
39a3(phal chen): don du chos yongasu btang zhing rim gror byas pas thugs su chud pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o/ /chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad yul du gyur pa'o/ /
39a4(phal chen): dus gsum thams cad la dgongs pa skad cig gis chags pa med par mkhyen cing thugasu chud pa'i yul dang ldan pa'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o/ /'jigs
39a5(phal chen): pa med par 'dul ba thams cad yul du gyur pa'o/ /thams cad kyi rjes su song zhing rnam par dag pa'i yul thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'o/ /sa mtshams med cing thug pa med pa'i mngon par shes pa rnam par
39a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi sems dang yid dang rnam par shes pa'i rnam pa dus gsum du brjod pa ma lus pa thams cad dgongs pa'i skad cig gis mkhyen cing thugs su chud pa'o/ /sems can gyi
39a7(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad la sa mtshams ma bcad pa'o/ /'jig rten gyi khams kyi rnam pa thams cad la mu med pa'o/ /dus gsum gyi rnam pa thams cad la mtha' yas pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung
39a8(phal chen): ba'i rnam pa thams cad la tshad med pa'o/ /shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad la lhag ma ma lus pa ste/ de dag thams cad lhag pa med par mngon par sangs rgyas pas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul
39b1(phal chen): dang rnam par 'phrul pas byung ba thams cad thugs su chud pa dang / mkhyen pa thams cad rgyun 'chad pa med de/ de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu byung ba'i skus/ mtha' dang
39b2(phal chen): dbus med par spyod pa yin/ chags pa med pa'i dgongs pas spyod pas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ thugs rje chen po'i sbyor bas dus thams cad du rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par chos bstan pa la spyod
39b3(phal chen): pas mtha' dang dbus myed pa spyod pa yin te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bcu pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i
39b4(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos rnams te/ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can
39b5(phal chen): thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsam gyi mi khyab cing dpag tu mi nus pa dag go/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi
39b6(phal chen): mnga' ba rnams te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dga' ldan gyi tshe/ ji srid par bzhugs nas 'pho ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zla ba bcur bltams pa bstan pa
39b7(phal chen): la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'byung bar dgyes pa'i dgongs pas mngon par 'byung ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub kyi
39b8(phal chen): shing drung du bzhugs nas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya ba la thogs pa la mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dgongs pa'i skad cig gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams
40a1(phal chen): cad mngon par sangs rgyas nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
40a2(phal chen): de bzhin du 'dul ba rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i tshul bzhin du dus la bab par bshad cing lung bstan pa la
40a3(phal chen): thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus la bab pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' yongs su grub pa rnams
40a4(phal chen): lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni skad cig gcig tu sems can thams cad kyis dri ba yongs su dris pa skad cig gcig gis lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ste/ kye rgyal ba'i
40a5(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' 'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos
40a6(phal chen): rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du ngan song dang bral bar 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du bsod nams yongasu rdzogs pa
40a7(phal chen): 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du dge ba'i rtsa ba la yongs su smin par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du mtho
40a8(phal chen): ris su skye ba yongs su dag pa thob par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams ni myur du yid gnyis dang / nem nur yang dag
40b1(phal chen): par bstsal ba thob par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas phyir mi ldog pa thob par 'gyur te/ sems can mos pa yangs
40b2(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba las byang chub tu sems ma bskyed pa rnams kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma
40b3(phal chen): thag tu skyon med par ma 'das pa dmyigs pa'i lta ba can rnams myur du skyon med par 'da' ba'i rgyu rab tu 'dzin to/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du
40b4(phal chen): 'jig rten dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang po rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du sgrib pa thams cad byang ba
40b5(phal chen): thob par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du snang ba thob cing mi 'jigs pa zhum pa med pa'i spobs pa rab tu rtsom te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu
40b6(phal chen): po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
40b7(phal chen): rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi sbyor bas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
40b8(phal chen): 'das rnams ni spyod pa rnam par dag pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pas kyang byang chub sems
41a1(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran par
41a2(phal chen): bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yang dag par bsgrubs pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mthar
41a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi tshangs par spyod pa la spyad pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i sgo nas kyang byang chub
41a4(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku tshad med mu med pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/
41a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa tshad med mu med pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
41a6(phal chen): ni stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjes su dran pa rnam
41a7(phal chen): par dag pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spyod pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos dbyings thams cad dang / dus gsum
41a8(phal chen): gyi sems can thams cad kyi sems sna tshogs dang / sems du ma dang spyod pa dang g.yo ba'i rgyud thams cad ma lus pa dgongs pa gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / dus gsum kyi sems can thams cad kyi las
41b1(phal chen): dang las kun nas blangs pa sna tshogs cha ma cho dgu rnam pa tha dad pas mngon par 'gro zhing 'jug par stsogs pa mang nyung dang / rnam par smin pa tha dad par ma lus par dgongs pa cig gis thugs su chud
41b2(phal chen): pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can gyi rigs sna tshogs dang / sems can gyi rigs du mi'i sems can ma lus pa thams cad 'dul ba'i dus ji bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul
41b3(phal chen): dang rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul gyi byin gyi brlabs yang dag par bstan pas ma lus pas thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / phyogs dra ba'i rgyud thams cad
41b4(phal chen): dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad kyi sems can thams cad gyi sems kyi mtshan ma bzung ba ste/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / skye ba dang rnam par dbye ba ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang /
41b5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba dang / mos pa ji lta ba dang 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med par skad cig du sangs rgyas bstan pa dang /
41b6(phal chen): rnam par dmigs par bya ba dang / byin gyis brlabs pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can pha rol kyi bsam pa la/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs
41b7(phal chen): yang dag par bstan pa ma lus pa thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du nye bar len pa med pa'i sangs rgyas nyid du 'gyur gdams ngag dang
41b8(phal chen): rjes su bstan pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi thams cad du 'gro ba dang / de dang der 'gro
42a1(phal chen): ba'i lam ma lus par dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa phyogs thams cad du btang ba'i
42a2(phal chen): tshul ma lus par dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyis mos pa dang / sems kyi tshad ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku
42a3(phal chen): kha dog mu myed pa dbyibs mtha' yas pa bstan pa ma lus par dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i

42a5(phal chen): tshad med bsam gyi mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can
42a6(phal chen): rnams la'ang skad cig gcig tu chos ston pa mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang skad cig gcig gis
42a7(phal chen): sems can gyi khams rnam pa dad pa rnams kyang bdag med pa'i mtha' la gnas par yongs su ston to/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi dus gsum la mnyam
42a8(phal chen): par bzhag kyang dgongs pa'i skad cig gcig gis cha shas la'ang mnyam par bzhag cing rnam par spyod do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi phyogs 'byam
42b1(phal chen): klas pa'i dra ba thams cad kyi zhing gi rgyud dang / rnam pa thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang mi zad pa'i zhing gi mtha' la'ang bzhugs shing rnam par spyod do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi
42b2(phal chen): d byings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi sku mu med pa la mnyam par bzhag kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi sku tshogs rnam par dmigs par yang dag par ston pa
42b3(phal chen): mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi yongs su rgyas par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang sems can thams cad kyi sems 'byung ba'i mdzod
42b4(phal chen): sna tshogs la yang mos pa dang yid la byed pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la rtag tu mnyam par
42b5(phal chen): bzhag kyang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i mtha'i mur thug pa la bzhugs pa yang yongs su mi gtong ngo / /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten thams cad

42b7(phal chen): c ad kyi 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa 'byam klas pa la rtag tu mnyam par gzhag kyang dgongs pa skad cig gis sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas mu med pa bstan pa rnam par bkod pa'i tshul
42b8(phal chen): mu med pa sangs rgyas bstan pa rgyun mi gcod do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du sgrib pa med par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang dgongs pa skad cig gis
43a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang rtogs par thugs su chud cing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa mu med pa pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes par bzhugs te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
43a2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin tshad med pa bsam gyi mi khyab pa rnams so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
43a3(phal chen): rnams kyi rnam par thar pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la
43a4(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo brjod du med pa'i brjod du med pa bskor ba yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang rdul shin tu phra ba cig la sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa
43a5(phal chen): yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar
43a6(phal chen): byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i zhing gi rgyud yongasu bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba
43a7(phal chen): gcig la 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa yongasu bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar
43a8(phal chen): b yung ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang la shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad yongs su bstan
43b1(phal chen): pa'i rnam par thar pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas rnams kyi rnam par thar pa'o/ /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam gyi mi khyab pa
43b2(phal chen): bstan pa'i le'u ste sum bcu dgu pa'o/ / //sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po lnga pa/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos mtshan rgya mtsho brjod du med pa'i don tu byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de
43b3(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la myi chen po'i mtshan chos kyi rgyan rin po che sna tshogs sum bcu rtsa gnyis mnga' bas de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu de ni 'khor yug nas/ 'od zer gyi dra ba shin tu 'byung zhing rgyas par
43b4(phal chen): gang ba ste/ de la myi chen po'i mtshan rin po che'i dang po dbu'i dbu tshams na rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgyal po'i las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang ba bkye ba/ dpal gyi yongs su rgyas shing
43b5(phal chen): yan lag dang nying lag thams cad nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin rnam par bkye ba yongs su 'khyil pa'i klong gi dbyibs kyis phyogs thams cad 'od kyis rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi
43b6(phal chen): dbu la 'phro ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor klog gi phreng ba lta bur 'byung bas/ phyogs mtshams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po byang chub tu bzhugs pa ston cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi nam mkha'i sprin kun tu 'das
43b7(phal chen): p as chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i rgyal po sna tshogs mdzod spu g.yas su yongs su 'khyil ba'i dbyibs las gser gyi kha dog bzang por 'od zer 'bar bar 'jig rten gyi
43b8(phal chen): khams su gyur pa'i 'od kyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gsal ba'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la rin po che'i
44a1(phal chen): 'od kyi klog g.yas phyogs su yongasu 'khyil ba/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams dang ye shes kyi sgron ma snang bas/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya
44a2(phal chen): mtsho thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi sprin rnam par bdal ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i mchog rnams la snang bas chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gser yid
44a3(phal chen): du 'ong ba'i sprin sna tshogs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / rab tu 'bar bas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par snang bar byas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi
44a4(phal chen): khyab pa snang bar bstan pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che bai dur+ya 'od zer dang / me tog gi mdog gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang bar rnam
44a5(phal chen): par 'phrul pa'i sprin nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po'i mtshan nyid lta bu'i dbu skra rin po che sna tshogs snang ba'i mtshan nyid kyi 'od chags pas/ phyogs thams cad rnam par snang bar byed pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sngon gyi dka' thub
44a6(phal chen): dang / dpal gyi ye shes las rnam pa de lta bur byung ba'i rin po che'i 'od zer rab tu bkye ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang / rin po che'i
44a7(phal chen): ' od gzer g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ci 'phro bas byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa rin po che'i cod pan gyi 'od de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rnam par rgyas pas 'jig rten
44a8(phal chen): g yi khams thams cad du rin po che'i 'od tshad myed par de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyis rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'
44b1(phal chen): ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che rnam par 'phrul pas/ nor bu rin po che rgya mtshos bkye ba'i 'od dang / 'od zer dri ma myed par rab tu
44b2(phal chen): 'phros pas byang chub sems dpa'i chos bstan pa rgya mtsho rnam par snang bar 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes kyi rgya mtsho shin tu yangs
44b3(phal chen): pas/ chos kyi dbyings kun tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi sprin 'byung ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la rin po che'i rgyal po sems kyi rgyal po dang / in
44b4(phal chen): tra nI la las 'od bkye ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pas 'jig rten gyi khams dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'od 'phro ba sgron ma'i sprin de bzhin gshegs pa thams
44b5(phal chen): c ad kyi yon tan rgya mtsho rab tu sgrogs pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad nga ro 'byin cing sangs rgyas kyi stobs yongs su dag pa rgya mtsho dang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho 'byin pa'i
44b6(phal chen): sbron shin tu yangs pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs dang / rin po che'i rgyal po bai dur+ya'i 'od zer rin po che thams cad
44b7(phal chen): kyi 'od zer kun tu 'byung ba'i dra ba mngon par 'phags pa las/ chos kyi lus dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / phyogs rgya mtshor de bzhin gshegs
44b8(phal chen): pa'i sa yang dag par ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi stobs chos kyi dbyings la mngon tu gyur pa rab tu ston par bzhugs pa/ sems can thams cad la yongs su ston pas/ de bzhin gshegs
45a1(phal chen): pa'i sa yang dag par 'phags shing yongs su dag la dri ma med pa yongs su mnan te/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kun tu snang ba'i rang bzhin rab tu bkye ba'i 'od zer dkyil 'khor gyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'
