50a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa 'og ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan tha dad pa'i mtshan nyid shin tu ston pas spos dang / rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i me tog sna tshogs thams cad
50a7(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od gzer rnam par snang ba kun tu 'phro ba'i sgron ma dri ma myed pa'i sprin yang dag par bstan pas/
50a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du rab tu gsal bas rnam par snang zhing de bzhin gshegs pa gdan seng ge'i khri pad mo'i snying po can dri ma myed pa la bzhugs pa'i sprin byang chub
50b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i rgya mtsho'i dbyings su rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi ri rab kyi mar mye rab tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa gong ma la de bzhin
50b2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che gser gyi 'od sna tshogs kun nas rnam par dag pa 'dzam bu chu klung gi rin po che'i rgyud kyis dra ba'i 'khor lo dang / rin po che'i me tog shin tu snang ba'i 'khor lo sna tshogs
50b3(phal chen): yongs su 'khyil pa/ chos kyi dbyings su gsung sgrog cing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa yongs su ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' yongs su smin par mdzad cing
50b4(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings su rgyan thams cad kyis gzugs brnyan gyi sprin zad mi shes pa'i kun tu mched par 'gyed pas chos rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang / rin po che thams cad
50b5(phal chen): kyi tshon du snang ba'i sangs rgyas nam mkha'i dbyings las gsung gi sgra 'byin pa/ chos kyi sgron ma'i 'od de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin du snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems
50b6(phal chen): kyi mtshams na/ de bzhin gshegs pa mtshan gcig par me tog gi mtshan dang / rgya mtsho'i sgo'i mtshan gyi sprin rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog du 'dal ba las/ rin po che'i 'od gzer
50b7(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu 'gyed cing bzhad mo 'dzum pas sangs rgyas kyi 'od nor bu rin po 'che'i 'od du 'phro ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil cing / chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa rin po che'i 'od gzer
50b8(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i khongs su chud pa'i snying po can gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi tshems kyi mtshams thams cad rgyas par gang bas/ skad cig tu 'od kyis rgyas par kun tu rgyu ba'i 'od gzer sangs rgyas
51a1(phal chen): kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho kun tu 'gyed pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgros la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang pad mo'i mdog dang
51a2(phal chen): 'od ltar snang ba chos kyi dbyings thams cad du mdangs rab tu snang bas dpal phun sum tshogs pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od gzer dang / mdangs kyis kun tu khyab par rnam par snang zhing gser dang
51a3(phal chen): pad mo'i mdog yongs su dag pas kun tu sbyangs pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi mdangs dang mdog tu snang ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mgur la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dung gi mgur
51a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od lam me/ lam mer yongs su snang bas/ mdog shin tu gsal zhing gzhi thams cad rin po che'i rgyal pos rnam par snang bar byas pas phyogs thams cad rnam par
51a5(phal chen): gsal ba'i 'od gzer rab tu 'gyed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar mdzad pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yas pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
51a6(phal chen): mtshan rin po che thams cad kyi 'od dang gser gyi kha dog rab tu 'phel bas/ pad mo'i mdog rnam par snang ba dang / rin po che'i 'od kyi dra ba rab tu snang ste/ kun tu gsal bar chos kyi dbyings
51a7(phal chen): snang bar mdzad cing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad khongs su chud pa'i sprin rab tu snang bas/ sangs rgyas rab tu mang ba thams cad snying por byas pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi gzhi
51a8(phal chen): dang ldan pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa'i dbus na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan shin tu 'phags shing yongs su rgyas la 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi 'od dang /
51b1(phal chen): mdog yongs su dag pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor lo rab tu snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings snang ba rin po che'i rgyal po mchog tu kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i
51b2(phal chen): sku phrag pa g.yon pa la sangs rgyas kyi dbu'i mdzod spu'i dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i gzhi las rin po che'i 'od gzer kyi dra ba sna tshogs shin tu bsgrubs pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang / pad mo'i mdog
51b3(phal chen): ltar gsal zhing bzang ba rab tu bkye bas chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pa'i 'od ston cing / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mdzod spu rin po
51b4(phal chen): che'i sprin kyi 'od rab tu snang ba bkye bas dpal rab tu 'bar zhing chos kyi dbyings rgyas par mdzad pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yas pa'i lhun la de bzhin gshegs
51b5(phal chen): pa'i mtshan mtshan nyid rnam par phye ba rin po che'i go ca 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser lta bu dpal thams cad kyis rgyas pas/ chos kyi dbyings kyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i 'od
51b6(phal chen): rnam par snang ba rin po che'i me tog spos kyi 'od 'phro bas/ zhing rgya mtsho thams cad rgyan rnam par phye bas brgyan te/ kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag
51b7(phal chen): pa g.yon pa'i lhun la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sgron ma 'od 'phro ba'i phung po'i sprin chos kyi dbyings kun tu mchod pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun yongs su khyab cing chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi'i
51b8(phal chen): rgyan tu gyur pas kun tu mched cing snang ba'i dbyings kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi thugs ka'i dpal gyi be'u la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan nyid rgya mtsho kun tu brgyan pas
52a1(phal chen): rab tu 'jam pa'i gzhi rin po che thams cad kyi mdog lta bur snang ba/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi tshad du 'od gzer gyi dkyil 'khor kun tu 'khyil pas yongs su dag cing / chos rgya mtsho'i
52a2(phal chen): gsung dbyangs dang ldan pa rin po che'i me tog shin tu rgyas pas rnam par brgyan te/ rin po che'i 'od gzer gyi mtshan gyi dbyings rgya mtsho la gnas pa'i dpal rgya mtsho kun gyi gzhung gi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /
52a3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u yi g.yas phyogs su 'dab chags na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa'i 'khor lo snang ba'i gzhi'i rgyan rin po che'i mig 'phrul gyi 'khor lo
52a4(phal chen): rnam par dag pa las sangs rgyas kyi sprin gyi lhun dri ma myed pas rab tu snang zhing phyogs thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings su 'od rnam par snang ba dpal gyi be'u dang / mtshams sbyor ba rab tu ston pa'i sprin ces
52a5(phal chen): bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u yi 'dab chags g.yon phyogs na/ byang chub sems dpa'i rin po che'i cod pan la snang ba shin tu 'phags pa'i sprin gyi lhun gyis lhun dri ma myed pas/
52a6(phal chen): thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston cing / chos rgya mtsho'i spyod pa rab tu bstan pas/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa dang /
52a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad rab tu ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u g.yas phyogs kyi 'og rol 'dab chags na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i
52a8(phal chen): me tog dang / rin po che'i mdzod spus rab tu brgyan pa'i rin po che'i 'khor lo rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma dri ma myed pa pad mo'i dbyings su 'jig rten gyi khams su ston pas me tog rgyas pa'i sprin
52b1(phal chen): ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u yi g.yon phyogs kyi 'og rol gyi 'dab chags na/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od sems kyi rgyal po'i snying po can rin po che'i rgyal po'i 'od
52b2(phal chen): gzer gyi 'khor lo dang / 'od rab tu bkye bas kun tu dri ma myed pa'i rgya mtsho shin tu 'phags pa'i khongs su sangs rgyas kyi tshul thams cad rab tu snang ba'i rin po che'i phung po ma lus par chud pa'i snying
52b3(phal chen): po can chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gser rab tu 'bar ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa dpal gyi be'u yi rtse mo la nam mkha'i dbyings su rin po che'i sgron ma spos rin po che'i rgyal po
52b4(phal chen): lus thams cad la snying po byang chub kyi 'od gzer rab tu 'bar zhing bai dUr+ya'i dkyil 'khor kyi sgrol ma la spos kyi 'phreng bas phyogs yangs pa thams cad rgyas par 'gengs shing / kun tu g.yas phyogs
52b5(phal chen): su 'khyil pa/ sangs rgyas kyi dpal gyi be'u rgya mtsho'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de'i 'og na rjes su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi be'u gnyis pa yod pa'i dbus na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan nyid
52b6(phal chen): kyi pad mo'i gzhi la ze ba byang chub sems dpa' g.yas phyogs su 'khor bar 'khod pa rab tu 'phags shing / yongs su dag la chos kyi dbyings rgya mtshor gsung sgrog pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od gzer gyi phung
52b7(phal chen): po'i snying po can rin po che'i rgyal pos shin tu brgyan pa rin po che'i 'od rab tu 'bar bas 'od gzer rnam par snang ba'i 'od kyi lhun dang ldan pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /rjes su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi be'u gsum
52b8(phal chen): pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan rgya mtshos yongs su gang ba'i rin po che rgya mtsho'i nang na zhing thams cad gzugs brnyan du 'khod par ston cing / byang chub sems dpa'i sprin gzhan dang
53a1(phal chen): gzhan mngon par phyung bas/ chos kyi dbyings rnam par snang ba'i sprin kun tu ston pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /rjes su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi be'u bzhi pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
53a2(phal chen): mtshan/ mtshan nyid kyis rnam pa rgya mtshos chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams dang rgyan thams cad snang bar 'jig rten gyi khams
53a3(phal chen): rgya mtshor/ 'od rab tu bkye ba'i 'od gzer snang ba phun sum tshogs pas rgyas par snang ba'i 'od gzer gyi sprin rin po che'i rgyal po'i 'khor lo g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba'i nyi ma rnam par snang ba dang /
53a4(phal chen): phreng ba kun tu byung zhing 'phags pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /dpal gyi be'u de'i 'og rol na chos thams cad kyi sgron ma'i dbyings dri ma med pa spos kyi me tog gi 'od gzer rab tu snang ba sangs rgyas rgya
53a5(phal chen): mtsho thams cad gyi thugs su 'dus pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rgya mtsho las chos kyi dbyings thams cad du/ chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad kyi gsung gi dbyangs kyi sprin zhes bya ba mnga'o/ /
53a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u bcu pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i phyogs thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi spyod pas mthu phyung zhing /
53a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'od yongs su dag pa dang / dri ma myed pa 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes rgya mtsho'i glong yongs su dag pa thams cad kyis
53a8(phal chen): zhing rgya mtsho rab tu brgyan cing klubs te/ rnam par 'god pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag gi mthil la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang
53b1(phal chen): ldan pa/ dbus rin po ches brgyan pa/ rin po che'i 'od gzer rnam par gsal ba'i 'od rnam par snang ba/ chos kyi dbyings su 'bar zhing 'khor lo g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba/ sangs rgyas
53b2(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i gzugs rnam par snang bas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od dang / dpal gyis rgyas par gang ba'i 'od gzer rin po che'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba sna tshogs thams cad lta bur 'jig
53b3(phal chen): rten gyi khams su chos kyi rgyan gyi sprin du snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag rin po che la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i rgyan gyi sprin zla ba'i 'od gzer kun tu 'byung bas
53b4(phal chen): n am mkha'i dbyings yongs su brgyan cing sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i gsung 'jig rten thams cad du sgrog pa rgya mtshos byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa rgya mtsho'i yang dag par brjod pa rgya mtsho'i

53b6(phal chen): can byang chub sems dpa' dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rin po che'i phung po mchog la gnas pa'i 'od phyogs thams cad kyi dbyings byang chub kyi shing rnam par bkod pas brgyan pa
53b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i sprin la/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi sku'i 'od snang ba myi g.yo ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'od 'phro ba rnam par
53b8(phal chen): snang ba dang / rin po che'i rlabs kyi 'od rnam par snang bas phyogs thams cad du sprul pa'i dra ba'i 'od kyi sprin rab tu bkye ste/ chos thams cad kyi spyod pa rgya mtsho la 'jug pas shin tu

54a2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i phyag la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i 'od kyi gzhi las blangs pa/ rgya mtsho'i snying po can gyi sprin sangs rgyas pad mos yongs su khyab pa'i mdog gi me tog shin tu rgyas

54b3(phal chen): phyag la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i sprin stug po'i glog gi phreng ba kun nas 'gyu bar rab tu 'dal ba/ zhing thams cad du snang zhing pad mo'i snying po can gyi gdan la sangs rgyas thams cad

54b7(phal chen): nyid rin po che yongs su dag pas/ chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa chu'i zla ba lta bur snang ba'i 'od kyi phung po'i snying po can rin po che'i rgyal po'i mtshan nyid kyis gzhi rab tu brgyan pa/ rin po
54b8(phal chen): che'i me tog gi 'dab ma'i mdog dang mtshon du snang bas/ rin po che thams cad kyi sgra mkhyen pa dang / zhing yongs su ston pa'i bskal pa dang / zhing gi glong rgya mtsho'i sprin ces bya ba
55a1(phal chen): mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag g.yon pa'i phyag sor la/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rnam par bkye ba'i rin po che'i mdzod chos kyi dbyings kyi klong thams cad du
55a2(phal chen): snang ba/ rin po che'i rgyal po mang po'i sprin mched de byung ba/ phyag sor gyi mtshan gyi gzhi rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'od gzer rnam pa tha dad pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag dra bar 'brel pa la/

55a6(phal chen): gzhan dang gzhan gyi 'od rin po che'i rgyal po'i gzhi nyi ma la sbyin pa sna tshogs kyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang ldan pa'i dkyil 'khor kun tu 'phel bas rnam par snang bar byas shing sprul pa/ chos
55a7(phal chen): kyi dbyings su snang ba rin po che thams cad kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba'i gnas sbubs su nub pa la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rim pa g.yas phyogs
55a8(phal chen): su 'khyil cing / 'od rab tu gsal ba dang ldan pa/ rin po che'i me tog chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i 'od nam mkha' lta bu rin po che thams cad kyi 'od du snang ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i

67a4(phal chen): yang zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'bras bu mngon par grub par gyur kyang / de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i sha'i mig gis sgrib pa myed par mthong ste/ lag na rin po che byang chub sems
67a5(phal chen): dpa'i sha'i mig las kyi rnam par smin pas yongs su grub pa des ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig brgya'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa sems skad cig gis mthong ste/ de ni 'jig rten

67a8(phal chen): bzang po'i 'od gzer bstan pa'i le'u ste/ bzhi bcu gcig pa'o// // sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po bdun pa/ de nas yang byang chub sems
67b1(phal chen): dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ni sems can gyi snod ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la dmyigs te rdul tsam zhig
67b2(phal chen): brjod du zad do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems can myi mkhas pa 'gyod pas kun nas non pa/ bdag dang bdag gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/ 'jig tshogs la shin tu chags pa/
67b3(phal chen): phyin ci log la rab tu rten pa/ the tsom la rab tu gzhol ba/ log par lta ba yongs su rtog pas byung ba rmongs pas bsgrubs pa/ 'khor ba'i rgyud du gzhol ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i lam dang myi ldan pa rnams
67b4(phal chen): kyi don du/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten du 'byung ngo / /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' gzhan la zhe sdang bskyed pa tsam du kha na ma tho ba che ba'i chos ni

67b6(phal chen): su 'dzin par 'gyur te/ brgya stong phrag bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' myi mthong ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /chos myi thos pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /'jig rten gyi khams kun nas
67b7(phal chen): nyon mongs par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /ngan song du gnas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /myi khom par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /nad mang ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /skur ba mang bar 'dzin par
67b8(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /ngang tshul myi gsal ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /brjed ngas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /blo chung ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /myig gi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /rna ba'i sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur

68a7(phal chen): byis pa'i chos la sten pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /theg pa dma' ba la mos pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /theg pa chen po la yid myi ches pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /bskal par gnas pas 'jig pa mang ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro/ /

72a5(phal chen): pa'i gsung gi dbyangs mngon par brjod pa'i sprin kyi char mngon par bab bo/ /'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag pa rnam pa brjod du med pa'i sprin kyi char mngon par bab bo/ /byang chub nye bar brten pa'i rnam pa brjod du
72a6(phal chen): med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo/ /'od gzer snang ba'i rnam pa brjod du myed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo/ /shin tu brtan pa'i byin kyi rlabs kyi char rnam pa brjod du med pa'ang mngon par bab ste/ ji ltar
72a7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams 'di'i gling bzhi bar de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi shing drung du de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i snying po byang chub la/ byang chub sems dpa' pho brang na bzhugs par snang ba de bzhin du
72a8(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa rgyas par gang bar bzhugs te/ chos bstan pa 'di yang thams cad du 'byung ngo / /sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang phyogs bcur de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par sangs rgyas
72b1(phal chen): pa'i chos nyid rab tu thob pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du myed pa phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin
72b2(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed kyang 'ongs par gyur te/ phyogs bcu bkang nas de dag 'di skad zer ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i smon lam lung bstan pa'i chos nyid brjod pa legs so/ /kye rgyal ba'i
72b3(phal chen): sras dag bdag cag kyang thams cad kun tu bzang po zhes bya bar mying mthun pa sha stag ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kun tu dpal zhes bya ba dag nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kun tu dpal gyi dbang phyug ces bya
72b4(phal chen): ba sha stag gi drung nas 'dir phyin te/ thams cad na 'di chos bstan pa 'di nyid sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'khor gyi rnam pa 'di lta bu dag tshig 'di dag dang yi ge 'di dag dang / go bar bya ba 'di dag dang / brjod pa 'di dag
72b5(phal chen): gis lhag cad myed par byung bar gyur te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag kyang dbang du gyur pa sha stag sangs rgyas kyis byin gyi rlabs kyis 'khor 'dir phyin to/ /ji ltar bdag cag 'khor 'dir phyin pa de bzhin du
72b6(phal chen): ' jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun gyi de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i gzhir byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis phyogs bcu bkang
72b7(phal chen): ste/ phyin par gyur to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos phyogs bcur bltas te/ chos kyi dbyings la rnam par bltas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rab tu brjod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
72b8(phal chen): pa mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i dbyings yongs su brjod pa dang / smon lam chen po'i dbyings kun tu grags par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams dang / bskal pa thams cad kyi grangs yongs su brjod pa dang /
73a1(phal chen): dus ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas 'byung ba bstan pa dang / sems can gyi khams dang dbang po ji ltar yongs su smin pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas byung ba mnyes par bya ba brjod pa dang / byin gyis
73a2(phal chen): brlabs pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas 'byung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa don yod pa yongs su brjod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa bzhin du gsal bar bya ba yang dag par bstan pa dang / byang chub
73a3(phal chen): sems dpa' mang po'i mthu chen po bstan pa dang / sems can thams cad la rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi sgras bskul ba byed cing dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs dang shugs dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis de'i tshe
73a4(phal chen): tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /thams cad shin tu dang sems kyis/ /sgrib pa ma lus thams cad rnam par bstsal gyis la/ /yon tan 'byung gnas 'jig rten gtso bo yi/ /smon lam dam pa bshad kyis
73a5(phal chen): mnyan par gyis/ /mkhas mchog skyes bu seng ge dag /spyad pa ci 'dra sngon spyad spyod par gyur pa rnams/ /byang chub sems dpa' gtso rnams kyi/ /spyod pa thams cad rim gyis brjod par bya/ /'di
73a6(phal chen): la dpe myed mchog rnams kyi/ /bskal pa'i grangs dang chos bstan pa/ /rgyal ba rnams kyi 'byung ba dag /yongs su brjod kyis dang ba'i yid kyis nyon/ /de dag sngon chad smon lam gyis/ /sems can ji ltar
73a7(phal chen): sdug bsngal rnams las grol bya zhes/ /sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir/ /'jig rten sgron ma skye bo rnams kyang mthong / /spyod pa ji ltar shes gyur te/ /gsung pa'i mchog rnams kun la mchod
73a8(phal chen): pa byas pas na/ /sangs rgyas mnyam pa nyid rnyed de/ /thams cad mkhyen nyid rab la mngon sangs rgyas/ /sngon gyi myi yi seng ge rnams/ /sangs rgyas phyogs bcur 'od snang rab tu 'bar mdzad cing / /
73b1(phal chen): 'od zer dra ba rab 'gyed pas/ /phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten snang mdzad mthong gyur nas/ /bdag cag rgyal ba'i yon tan gyis/ /brgyan pa'i 'jig rten sgron ma'i dam par gyur byas te/ /stobs bcu mnga'
73b2(phal chen): ba kun mkhyen par/ /myi yi seng ge bya zhes smon lam 'debs/ /nged kyis sems can thams cad kyi/ /'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug rab tu 'bar gyur pa'i/ /sdug bsngal rnams las rab bgrol te/ /
73b3(phal chen): ngan song thams cad yongs su gcod bya zhes/ /'di 'dra'i smon lam rdzogs byas te/ /de nas dpa' ba chen po spyod pa rab la spyod/ /blo brtan phyir ldog myi 'gyur ba/ /stobs bcu rnams kyi chags med rab tu
73b4(phal chen): 'thob/ /skyes bu seng ge gang rnams kyi/ /'di 'dra'i smon lam sngar btab phyir ldog myi 'gyur ba/ /'jig rten rnams ni spyod mdzad pa/ /de dag don yod spyod pa brjod par bya/ /bskal pa bzang po gcig la
73b5(phal chen): yang / /sangs rgyas stong grangs tshang bar kun kyang 'byung gyur te/ /kun tu gzigs pa gang brjod pa/ /de dag rim gyis bshad pa 'di 'dra'o/ /bskal pa bzang po gcig bzhin du/ /brjod du myed pa'i bskal pa khrag
73b6(phal chen): khrig de bzhin te/ /sangs rgyas ma byon de dag gi/ /bzang po'i spyod pa bdag gis bstan par bya/ /zhing rgyud gcig po ji bzhin du/ /brjod du myed pa'i zhing rnams thams cad kun bzung ste/ /ma byon stobs
73b7(phal chen): bcu'i skyon myed pa'i/ /spyod pa thams cad de bzhin bshad par bya/ /rgyal ba gang dag gang 'byung dang / /ci mtshan de'i smon lam rnam pa ci 'dra dang / /rgyal ba gang gis gang gis lung / /bstan mdzad
73b8(phal chen): mkhas pa'i sku tshe ji tsam dang / /chos kyi rnam pa dge ba ni/ /gang gis bsgrubs te dam pa brnyes par gyur pa dang / /'jig rten ji ltar btul ba dang / /rgyal ba rnams kyi dam chos cir gnas dang / /
74a1(phal chen): rnam dag zhing yang ci 'dra dang / /sems can rnam par dag dang chos kyi 'khor lo dang / /bstan pa'i dus dang dus myin dang / /de las gang zag rnam par dag 'gyur dang / /sems can rnams kyi las
74a2(phal chen): gang dang / /spyod pa gang dang rnam grol ji 'drar 'gyur ba dang / /dbang po rno rtul bar ma dang / /spyod mchog sems can 'dul ba'ang bstan par bya/ /'di 'dra'i shes par 'jug pa la/ /spyod pa'i dam pa rnams
74a3(phal chen): kyis rab tu zhugs gyur cing / /bzang po'i 'byung gnas spyod pa dang / /'gro kun ye shes 'khor lo spyod zhugs pa/ /lus kyi las la chags med cing / /ngag la chags myed sgra dbyangs thams cad rnam dag
74a4(phal chen): la/ /sems spyod chags pa myed pa yis/ /dus gsum ma lus rgyas par khyab par byed/ /'di 'dra kun tu bzang po yi/ /spyod pa'i mchog la pha rol phyin pa thob gyur pa/ /brjod du myed pa'i dkyil 'khor
74a5(phal chen): rnams/ /chos dbyings kun tu rab tu brjod par byed/ /ma 'ongs dus kyi bskal pa dang / /'byam klas zhing rnams brjod du med pa thams cad kyang / /skad cig sems kyis rab tu shes/ /chos nyid de
74a6(phal chen): la rnam par rtog pa myed/ /gang rnams spyod pa'i sa 'di la/ /spyod pa'i dam pas rjes su zhugs par gyur pa rnams/ /byang chub sems dpa' mchog rnams kyi/ /yon tan spyod pa phyogs tsam bshad par
74a7(phal chen): bya/ /mtha' dang dbus myed ye shes can/ /stobs bcu rnams kyi spyod yul mchog la zhugs gyur pa/ /thams cad shes byed mkhas pa'i rnams/ /mi ldog spyod pas rab tu zhugs gyur cing / /'od byed
74a8(phal chen): blo gros dam pa dang / /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam mchog la zhugs gyur pa/ /dpe zla myed pa de dag gi/ /ye shes tshul dang spyod pa brjod par bya/ /rdul phran gcig gi cha shas la/ /'jig rten khams
74b1(phal chen): rnams ji snyed de dag shes pa dang / /spyod pa rgya che thos gyur na/ /'jig rten de dag thams cad mos par 'gyur/ /rdul phran gcig la ji lta ba/ /de bzhin rdul phran thams cad ma lus gzung byas ste/ /
74b2(phal chen): ye shes bzang po de dag ni/ /'jig rten khams la 'jug pa bsam mi khyab/ /de dag dus kyi rnam pa la 'ang / /rdul phran gcig gi khyon kyi cha la yang dag 'jug /rdul phran gcig la de bzhin du/ /zhing
74b3(phal chen): yangs rnam pa tha dad kun la 'jug / rdul phran thams cad re re la/ /zhing rnams brjod du myed pa mang po 'dzud pa byed/ /rnam pa tha dad du ma dang / /gcig dang tshad med de bzhin rab tu shes/ /ji
74b4(phal chen): snyed ci 'ang ma lus pa'i/ /chos dbyings gzung ba thams cad yang dag gzung byed cing / /mtshan nyid tha dad sna tshogs te/ /sems can grangs kyi skal pa rgyud myi mnyam/ /'jig rten phra bar 'jug
74b5(phal chen): pa la/ /phra la shin tu gzhol bas phra bar 'jug byas te/ /brjod du med par bstan pa yi/ /bskal pa thams cad ma lus 'dzud pa byed/ /de dag ring dang thung ba dang / /dus kyi skad cig sems
74b6(phal chen): la skal ba mi 'thun shes/ /shes spyod myi mnyam ma yin pa'i/ /shes pas de dag thams cad khong du chud/ /yangs dang yangs myin mkhas pas ni/ /'jig rten zab mo rnams la rab tu 'jug
74b7(phal chen): par byed/ /lus la zhing rnams de shes te/ /zhing la 'ang de bzhin gcig myin lus 'dzud do/ /phyogs rnams bcu pa thams cad du/ /phyogs rnams kun la 'jug cing skad cig du ma dang / /
74b8(phal chen): 'jig rten khams rnams 'byam klas la/ /tshad med gzi brjid ldan pa rab tu 'jug /gang yang zhing rnams mtha' yas shing / /dbus myed gzung ba byas shing dus kyi dbyings su 'dzud/ /
75a1(phal chen): zhing gi rgyud la mkhas pa'i rnams/ /shes dang ldan pas ye shes rab tu 'byung / /bzang po'i yon tan ldan pa'i rnams/ /phyogs dang 'jig rten khams kyi rgyud du gyur pa dag /ji snyed
75a2(phal chen): yod pa de 'jug ste/ /brjod du med pa de dag rab tu shes/ /zhing dang zhing gi sa rnams kyi/ /brjod du myed pa'i zhing rnams kun kyang rab tu mthong / /de dag tshul yang rab tu shes las rnams/ gang
75a3(phal chen): gis sbyangs pa 'ang khong du chud/ /gang yang zhing rnams du ma dag /las rnams khrag khrig kun kyis kun nas nyon mongs par/ /'gro bas kun tu bsgrubs byas pa/ /de dag thams cad rgyud kyang ci 'dra
75a4(phal chen): shes/ /brjod du myed pa yangs pa'i rnams/ /zhing gcig bstan pas de dag yongs su shes par 'gyur/ /de 'dra'i zhing la 'jug pa dang / /gang la grangs myed de dag kun la 'jug /'jig rten khams ni
75a5(phal chen): gcig la yang / /'jig rten khams thams cad yang dag 'dzud pa byed/ /'jig rten gcig tu dgongs myi 'gyur/ /'jig rten khams rnams de bzhin 'dres myi 'gyur/ /spyi'u tshugs rnams dang gong
75a6(phal chen): ma'i rnams/ /bla dang 'og gi sa rnams yongs su gzung byas te/ /'gro ba'i rnam par mying thogs pa/ /'jig rten kun la 'jug cing rab tu shes/ /snrel bzhir rgyu ba'i rgyud rnams dang / /zhing rnams
75a7(phal chen): mtha' yas mtha' dang dbus yod ma yin pa/ /sna tshogs yangs pa rab tu shes/ /rnam pa gcig shes rnam pa tha dad shes/ /zhing gi grangs rnams rab tu shes/ /ye shes chags myed mtha'
75a8(phal chen): ldan kun kyi grangs rnams kyang / /bzang po'i theg pa spyod pa yis/ /rgyal sras kun tu bzang rnams rab tu shes/ /'jig rten thams cad sprul pa dang / /sems can rnam par sprul dang de bzhin
75b1(phal chen): zhing sprul dang / /chos rnams sprul pa'i tshul shes pa/ /sangs rgyas sprul pa'i pha rol phyin pa rnams/ /'jig rten phra zhing zab pa dang / /yangs shing sna tshogs yangs pas cho ma cho dgu rnams/ /sna
75b2(phal chen): tshogs tha dad rnam bstsags pa/ /las kyi rnam smin gnas pa'i 'jig rten rnams/ rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pa yis/ /chos dbyings 'jug par bya la shin tu bslabs pa yi/ /rgyal sras mtha' dang
75b3(phal chen): dbus myed pa/ /phyogs bcu thams cad ma lus 'gengs pa byed/ /'jig rten khams rnams de dag gi/ /mying ni bskal pa sems can snyed kyis mthar thug cing / /zad par brjod par myi nus te/ /
75b4(phal chen): mying bshad gal te sangs rgyas gsung na gsung / /'jig rten mgon po rnams kyi yang / /mtshan rnams mtshan nyid mi 'thun rnam pa sna tshogs mtshan/ /bskal pa brjod myed zad byas kyang / /
75b5(phal chen): mtshan rnams gcig nas gcig brgyud mthar thug myed/ /'on kyang dman pa'i sems myed par/ /mkhas pa rnams ni dus gsum bde gshegs sangs rgyas phyir/ /chos kyi dbyings las byung ba
75b6(phal chen): ste/ /sangs rgyas ye shes sa la 'ang rab tu zhugs/ /dran pas chags med dag pa ste/ /chags med yid dang ldan zhing blo gros mtha' yas pas/ /ye shes blo gros mchog ldan pa/ /chos dbyings
75b7(phal chen): bshad la pha rol phyin pa thob/ /gang gis 'jig rten khams kyi rnams/ /yangs dang phra ba rnam pa sna tshogs shes gyur cing / /der ni 'das pa'i dus rnams la/ /sems gcig bskyed pas rab tu 'jug
75b8(phal chen): pa byed/ /myi yi seng ge de dag tu/ /sangs rgyas spyod pa sna tshogs rnam par chags myed par/ /byang chub mchog tu sangs rgyas shing / /rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad ston pa mdzad/ /de bzhin ma
76a1(phal chen): 'ongs dus rnams kyi/ /rjes su gang byon de yi bskal pa ci 'dra dang / /de la myi yi seng ge gang / /skye bar 'gyur ba de dag kun kyang shes/ /smon lam spyod pa ci 'dra dang / /spyod yul gang
76a2(phal chen): rnams sgom pa gang gis grub gyur cing / /sgrub pa'i rnam pa ci 'dra bas/ /bskal pa gang la byang chub 'tshang rgya dang / /de dag 'khor kyang khong du chud/ /sku tshe'i tshad dang sems can 'du ba ci 'dra dang / /
76a3(phal chen): chos kyi sgo mo gang zhig gis/ /'gro bar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba shes/ /de ltar kun tu bzang po'i ye shes mchog gis bsgrub pa'i spyod pa'i sa gnas shing / /de dag thams cad rab tu shes/ /
76a4(phal chen): de ni 'gro gtso kun gyi 'byung gnas yin/ /da ltar byung ba gzung byas shing / /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad 'dab chags ma lus par/ /'jig rten khams rnams dag tu 'jug /de bzhin
76a5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings rnams rab tu shes/ /de na myi yi gtso bo rnams/ /dgra las rgyal zhing thams cad gzigs pa ji snyed pa/ /myi thub rgol ba dpa' bo rnams/ /chos kyi mnga' la pha rol phyin brnyes pa/ /
76a6(phal chen): de dag 'khor kyang rab tu shes/ /sems can 'dul dang zhing rnams rnam par dag pa dang / /rgyal ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa rnams/ /sems dpas bskal pa yangs pa zad par byed/ /skyes bu'i mchog
76a7(phal chen): rnams 'dul mdzad cing / /'jig rten mchog du phyin pa'i byin brlabs dam pa la/ /myi zad mdzod kyi shes yangs pas/ /ye shes tshul la mkhas pa rab tu 'jug /chags med myig gis blta ba
76a8(phal chen): dang / /chags med rna ba mngon par sgrub pa bsgrub byed cing / /chags pa myed pa'i lus yangs dang / /yangs pa'i lces kyang 'jig rten tshim par byed/ /dam pa'i sems la chags myed de/ /bsam pa
76b1(phal chen): kun tu rnam yangs rnam par dag dang ldan/ /ye shes 'byung gnas bdag nyid de/ /dus gsum sems rnams ma lus des khyab bo/ /sprul pa'i pha rol phyin thob cing / /zhing rnams sprul pa'i brlabs par
76b2(phal chen): bya la bslab pa'i rnams/ /sems can sprul la mkhas pa dag /sprul pa sprul pas 'jig rten 'dul ba byed/ /'du shes rnam pa du ma ste/ /des ni 'jig rten sna tshogs du ma lus rnams bris/ /de dag
76b3(phal chen): thams cad rab tu shes/ /sangs rgyas ye shes tshul la rab tu 'jug /'khor rnams brjod du myed pa dag /sangs rgyas chos rnams re re dag la yod pa'i rnams/ /kun la 'jug cing mthong bar byed/ /
76b4(phal chen): sems can rnam par 'dul ba'i mtha' 'ang myed/ /ye shes zab mo mthong bas na/ /ye shes nyi ma shin tu gsal bar shar gyur pa'i/ /phyir myi ldog pa'i spyod pa la/ /'jig rten 'byam klas kun tu
76b5(phal chen): 'jug pa byed/ /ji lta'i tshul du zhugs gyur cing / /'jig rten 'di dag thams cad rnam par bkod 'dra bar/ /sems can tshul bzhin rab tu 'phags/ /khams gsum thams cad myig yor tshul
76b6(phal chen): 'drar shes/ /'on kyang rtog dang rnam rtog myed/ /'jig rten mtha' dang dbus myed kun la rtog myi byed/ /rtog dang rtog myed mkhas pa ste/ /rtog pa'i shes pas rnam par rtog pa myed/ /bskal pa brjod
76b7(phal chen): du myed pa rnams/ /sems bskyed gcig la yang dag 'du bar 'jug byed cing / /'jig rten myi khom 'di mthong nas/ /skad cig sems kyis thams cad shes par byed/ /brjod du myed pa'i zhing rnams kyang / /
76b8(phal chen): sems bskyed gcig gis thams cad yongs su 'da' bar byed/ /bskal pa brjod med zad byed kyang / /skra rtse'i cha shas gcig las g.yo ba myed/ /bskal pa brjod du med pa dag /nyi ma gcig dang
77a1(phal chen): yid tsam gcig tu 'dzud byed kyang / /ring dang thung la gzhol ba myed/ /skad cig gcig la 'jug pa'i pha rol phyin/ /sems kyi rnam pa 'jig rten kun/ /'jig rten rnam pa sems can kun
77a2(phal chen): gyi sems yin no/ /rnam pa gnyis kyi grangs su zhugs/ /'on kyang de dag mi gnyis rtog pa myed/ /sgyu ma'i rnam pa 'jig rten te/ /sems can zhing dang sangs rgyas chos kyang de bzhin no/ /'on kyang 'jig
77a3(phal chen): rten mgon po rnams/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams kun la gcig tu snyoms/ /lus rnams brjod du myed pa yis/ /phyogs bcu thams cad rgyas par bkang zhing yongs su ston/ /'on kyang lus la gzhol ba
77a4(phal chen): myed/ /chos nyid rten pa gnas med rab tu shes/ /'on kyang myi yi seng ge rnams/ /gnyis la gnas pa'i shes pas byung ba ma yin te/ /myi gnyis pa la 'ang gnas pa med/ /gnyis dang gnyis myed chos
77a5(phal chen): rnams rab tu shes/ /ji ltar smyig rgyu rab rib dang / /myig yor sgra snyan de bzhin rmyi lam 'dra ba dang / /rmi lam rnam pa sprul pa ltar/ /'gro ba thams cad ma lus rab tu shes/ /de ltar spyod yul nyams myed
77a6(phal chen): pas/ /sangs rgyas kun kyi rigs kyi rjes su 'byung ba yin/ /kun tu bzang po'i ye shes dang / /chos kyi dbyings la shin tu bdal ba yin/ /snying rje chen po mtha' yas kyang / /sems can myed dang mnyam
77a7(phal chen): par zhing rnams thams cad sgom/ /sngon nas nyon mongs nyams myed pa'i/ /bsam pa dag pas 'jig rten kun tu 'gro/ /myi zad mkha' ltar rnam par dag pa yi/ /rgya che shin tu yangs pa'i sa la rab tu
77a8(phal chen): zhugs/ /gsung ba'i seng ge thams cad kyi/ /tshul gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rjes su dran/ /'jig rten rab tu spros pa la/ /smon lam tshad myed yongs su gdab pa byas pas na/ /de dag spyod pa yongs
77b1(phal chen): su dag / 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad rgyas par khyab byas pa/ /sangs rgyas rnams dang rgyal sras dang / /de bzhin sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos rnams thams cad dang / /'jig rten rnams dang 'jig rten
77b2(phal chen): chos/ /chags med tha dad myed pa'i tshul du shes/ /chos kyi sku yi snying po can/ /de yi lus la 'jig rten thams cad gzung byas shing / /'jig rten de yi lus yin yang / /'jig rten kun kyi de la gos pa myed/ /
77b3(phal chen): ji ltar dang ba'i chu gsal la/ /gzugs brnyan yongasu snang yang der song 'phos pa myed/ /de bzhin 'jig rten thams cad kyi/ /rjes su lus 'gro der song 'phos pa myed/ /ji ltar 'jig rten thams cad kyi/ /
77b4(phal chen): gos pa med cing 'jig rten yongs su dag pas na/ /lus ni mkha' dang 'dra ba ste/ /de yi lus rnams gang la 'ang skyes pa myed/ /myi zad pa yi lus shes pas/ /de ni nam yang skyes shing 'gags pa myed pa ste/ /
77b5(phal chen): rtag dang myi rtag ma yin par/ /'jig rten kun la 'ang rnam par dmyigs pa byed/ /lta ba'i rnam pa rab tu 'gags/ /brtan pa de dag yang dag blta ba ston pa byed/ /bdag gi myed cing gnas pa myed/ /len pa myed cing
77b6(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam/ /ji ltar sgyu mkhan mkhas pas zhing / /sna tshogs mtshan nyid rnam pa tha dad gshegs 'phrul byed/ /'on kyang de la 'gro ba myed/ /gang du 'ang 'gro ba de bzhin myi dmyigs so/ /sgyu ma
77b7(phal chen): tshad myed ma yin te/ /sgyu ma tshad kyis dmyigs par bya ba'ang ma yin no/ /tshad myed tshad dang ldan par yang / /tshogs kyi dbus su ston pa rab tu byed/ /de bzhin rtogs pa'i blo ldan pa/ /sangs rgyas kun kyi dge
77b8(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba rnams las byung / /sems ni tshad yod ma yin te/ /tshad myed pa la gnas pa 'ang de dag myin/ /'du shes rnam pa gcig myin te/ /de dag tshad med pa dang tshad dang ldan pa ston/ /lam gyi rgyud dang
78a1(phal chen): 'brel pa myed/ /tshad myed rnams la gnas pa 'ang de bzhin myed/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams zab pa ste/ /shin tu yangs pas zab cing zhi bas de bzhin zab/ /zab mo sna tshogs rgyud rnams dang / /
78a2(phal chen): mtha' yas zab pa rnams kyang rab tu shes/ /ye shes bzang po rmongs pa myed/ /rgyud la dri ma myed pas bsam pa rnam par dag /byin kyis rlob la mkhas pas na/ /srog chags bye ba shin tu dga' bar
78a3(phal chen): byed/ /dge bar byed pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams/ /rab tu brjod cing dge dang myi dge rnam par ston/ /gnas la mngon par ma chags pas/ /chos kyi dbyings rnams kun tu rab tu rgyu/ /sems can myed mthar phyin
78a4(phal chen): gyur kyang / /'jig rten thams cad ma lus par/ /rnam par sangs rgyas mya ngan gar myi 'da'/ /chos rnams bgrang ba'i tshul la mkhas/ /sems can bgrang tshul shes kyang grangs la skyes pa myed/ /
78a5(phal chen): chos kyi sprin chen char 'bebs shing / /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad snang bar byed/ /sangs rgyas byang chub ma lus la/ /sems bskyed gcig gis de dag rab tu 'jug /de dag phyir ldog myed
78a6(phal chen): pa ste/ /sems can kun kyi khams las phyir myi ldog /sangs rgyas sku ni thob gyur kyang / /chos rnams 'di dag lus yod ma yin rab tu shes/ /lus rnams kun gyi tshul la mkhas/ /lus kyis rnam
78a7(phal chen): phye 'jig rten rab tu shes/ /sems can kun tu rgyu ba dang / /bskal pa rnams dang zhing la pha rol phyin pa thob/ /phyogs rnams rgya mtshor ye shes rgya mtsho'i tshul la mkhas pas zhugs/ /lus rnams
78a8(phal chen): thams cad re re las/ /sems can kun kyi lus rnams sna tshogs ji snyed dang / /sangs rgyas sku ni mtha' yas pa/ /ye shes shin tu yangs pa de ston to/ /skad cig gcig gi dus tshul la/ /
78b1(phal chen): mi yi gtso bo mang po 'byung ba rab tu shes/ /bskal pa mang po brjod myed du/ /myi yi seng ge bgrang bas zad myi 'gyur/ /de dag mya ngan 'da' ba yang / /skad cig gcig la tshad myed shin tu yangs pa
78b2(phal chen): 'byung / /ring bsrel rnam dbye mang po yang / /ye shes dri med phra bas ston pa byed/ /de bzhin ma 'ongs dus kyi yang / /myi yi seng ge mtha' yas smon lam 'debs pa'i rnams/ /byang chub dri med
78b3(phal chen): sems bskyed pa/ /ye shes yangs shing shin tu phra bas shes/ /bzang po'i spyod la gnas bcas shing / /de bzhin dus gsum gshegs pa'i sems can gtso bo rnams/ /de snyed skyes par 'gyur pa dag /
78b4(phal chen): de dag thams cad ma lus rab tu shes/ /de ltar rab tu shes pas na/ /mtha' dang dbus med spyod pa'i sa dang de bzhin du/ /ye shes 'byung gnas blo gros la/ /ye shes 'khor lo'i spyod pas phyir myi ldog /
78b5(phal chen): ye shes phra mo rab yangs pa/ /stobs bcu rnams kyi spyod yul mchog la de dag zhugs/ /bzang po rtogs pa'i blo can rnams/ /phyir myi ldog la 'jug pa brjod byas na/ /sangs rgyas rgyal ba thams
78b6(phal chen): cad kyi/ /yang dag gzhol bar bya la de dag zhugs pas na/ /spyod las phyir ldog myed pa ste/ /byang chub dam pa zhi bar 'tshang rgya yang / /de 'dra'i sems rgyud gcig la yang / /mtha' dang dbus myed sems
78b7(phal chen): rnams yang dag 'dzud pa byed/ /shin tu yangs pa'i tshad med las/ /'du shes de dang de la yang dag bsgrub/ /nyon mongs myed dang nyon mongs dang / /slob dang myi slob sems kyang de bzhin rab tu shes/ /
78b8(phal chen): sems rgyud de dag re re la'ang / /sems rnams brjod du med pa mngon 'tshang rgya/ /gcig dang gnyis su shes pa myed/ /yang dag yongs su 'dres par 'gyur ba 'ang myed pa ste/ /so so'i 'du shes rnam
79a1(phal chen): pa la/ /sems can de dag skyes par gyur pa yin/ /'di na 'dug par mthong gyur kyang / /sems can brjod myed gzhan dang gzhan sems ldan pa'i rnams/ /gzhan gyi zhing phyir 'du shes kyang / /
79a2(phal chen): 'jig rten sna tshogs rnams la rab tu skye/ 'di 'dra'i tshul la 'jug pa la/ /spyod pa'i mchog gi rjes su zhugs par gyur pa rnams/ /kun tu bzang po'i mying thob ste/ /'jig rten mgon po kun kyi rjes su
79a3(phal chen): skyes/ /sems can bye ba la la ni/ /ngan song 'grangs pa'i mying thogs mtho ris 'du shes 'gyur/ /la la mtho ris sa rnams kyi/ /rnam pa kun la ngan song 'du shes 'gyur/ /'jig rten myi mtshungs skal
79a4(phal chen): ba ltos/ /rnam pa tha dad las kyi sa las rab tu skyes/ /'du shes rnam pa mtha' yas te/ /gcig myin yang la 'jig rten rab tu 'jug /'jig rten khams rnams thams cad kyi/ /'du shes dra
79a5(phal chen): ba skal pa myi mnyam rab tu shes/ /myig 'phrul sgyu ma'i tshul gyis na/ /skad cig gcig gis sems kyis rab tu gzhol/ /de bzhin dbang po rnams la ste/ /mig gi skye mched rna ba sna yi skye
79a6(phal chen): mched dang / /lce dang lus dang yid la yang / /'jig rten rnam pa tha dad 'du shes 'jug /myig rnams re re'i yul la yang / /mtha' dang dbus myed myig rnams rab tu 'dzud pa byed/ /rnam pa tha
79a7(phal chen): dad du ma ste/ /tshad myed kun la'ang zhen par 'gyur ba med/ /'on kyang phan tshun gcig gis gcig /bde zhing gnod par 'gyur ba de dag kun na myed/ /bdag bdag so so'i las kyi rnams/ /ji ltar
79a8(phal chen): bstsags pa'i tshul bzhin nyams su myong / /bzang zhes bya ba de dag kun/ /tshad myed stobs dang ye shes sa yi shes rab kyis/ /'byam klas myig rnams thams cad la/ /rab tu zhugs pas
79b1(phal chen): shin tu rtogs pa yin/ /de bzhin 'jig rten thams cad kyang / /thams cad ma lus rnam pa thams cad 'jig tshul du/ thams cad shin tu shes gyur kyang / /rgya chen spyod pas mya ngan mi 'da'o/ /
79b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas shin tu bstan pa dang / /sems can bstan dang de bzhin zhing rnams bstan pa dang / /dus rnams shin tu bstan pa dang / /bstan pa sna tshogs rnam pa kun kyang shes/ /la la 'di la 'das
79b3(phal chen): gyur kyang / /gzhan dang gzhan rnams ma 'ongs dus la gnas pa yin/ /'on kyang ma 'ongs dus kyi rnams/ /la las da ltar byung bar rab tu shes/ /de 'dra'i tshul can gcig myin pa'i/ /'jig rten
79b4(phal chen): mtshan nyid tha dad thams cad rab tu shes/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid tshul gyi/ /sangs rgyas ye shes kun tu mtha' 'ang yas/ /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ /sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba
79b5(phal chen): las/ kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa bstan pa'i le'u ste/ bzhi bcu gnyis pa'o// // sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po brgyad pa/ bcom ldan 'das ye shes
79b6(phal chen): chen pos rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i dgongs pa mnga' ba 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang / sku gcig pa'i mnyam pa nyid brnyes pa/ sangs rgyas thams
79b7(phal chen): cad kyi spyod pa mnyam pa nyid dang ldan pa/ chags pa med pa'i spyod yul mngon par mkhyen pa/ ye shes kyi rang bzhin gyi chos kyi sku mnga' ba/ mtshan nyid yod nas med pa'i chos la rten pa/ chos kyi
79b8(phal chen): dbyings myi gnyis pa'i spyod yul gyi yang dag par spyod pa/ mtha' dang dbus myed cing mtshungs pa'i mngon par 'tshang rgya ba brnyes pa/ rnam par thar pa sgrib pa myed pa'i spyod yul la shin tu dgyes
80a1(phal chen): pa/ chos kyi sku nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa mnga' ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyi pho brang khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzhal myed khang de bzhin gshegs pa
80a2(phal chen): bzhugs pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi snying po can/ 'od kun nas 'byung ba rgyan chen po dang ldan la/ 'od dang zhing gsal ba/ rnam par snang ba'i snying po can sangs rgyas skye ba chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus myed
80a3(phal chen): pa'i gnas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus las byung ba/ gzhi 'od zer gyi rnam par brgyan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus rang bzhin du gnas pas rab tu bsgrub pa/ chos chen po'i gzhir gyur
80a4(phal chen): pa/ chos kyi dbyings kun tu rgyas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od dang ldan pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa/ ye shes kyi yul yang dag pa'i mtha' spyod yul chags pa med pas rnam
80a5(phal chen): par gsal ba na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin po che bzang po'i pad mo chen po rang rang gi smon lam gyi byung ba'i dbus kyi snying po la 'khod pa'i kun kyang tshe gcig gis thogs pa/
80a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang gzhan nas phyin pa/ ye shes chen po rnam par phye ba'i spyod yul la bzhol ba/ chos kyi dbyings tha myi dad pa'i gzhi mnyam pa nyid la zhugs pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings gzhi myed
80a7(phal chen): cing / mtha' dang dbus myed pa la rnam par spyad pa/ chos thams cad 'byung ba med cing / mngon par grub pa med pa mngon du byas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus las ma g.yos par thams cad
80a8(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes rab tu thob pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du kun gyis brjod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes las mngon du byung ba/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub mngon sum
80b1(phal chen): du gyur pa'i ye shes snang ba thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul rgyun ma chad pa/ ye shes kyi rang bzhin chos kyi lus gcig cing tha myi dad pas/ gzugs kyi lus mtha' yas pa'i sgo kun tu ston pa/ chos kyi
80b2(phal chen): dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa la 'jug pa shin tu shes pa/ sems can kyi khams su rnam par spyod pa las phyir myi ldog pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi dbyings dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' mnyam pa nyid thob
80b3(phal chen): pas sprul pa mngon par sgrub pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad dang / sngon lhan cig tu skyes shing dge ba'i rtsa ba bstsags pa sha stag la 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu
80b4(phal chen): bzang po dang / kun tu grags pa'i dbang phyug rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal dang / rdo rje dpal gyi rgyal mtshan dang / rnam par grol ba sgrib pa med pa'i zla ba dang / nyi ma'i 'od zer
80b5(phal chen): dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / mngon par shes pa chen pos rnam par 'phrul pa'i blo dang / 'od dri ma med pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid 'od gzer gyi rgyal po dang / blo gros rgya mtsho'i mchog 'dzin cing blo la rnam
80b6(phal chen): par rtse ba/ gsal bas mngon par shes pa'i dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po stobs bcus myi 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen pos rnam par rtse bas mngon par shes
80b7(phal chen): pa dang / de dag las stsogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs
80b8(phal chen): so/ /de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi mdzod spu nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i 'od gzer kyi 'khor bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa mang po'i 'od gzer dang ldan pa byung ste/
81a1(phal chen): des 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad du ma lus par snang bar byas/ 'jig rten g.yas phyogs su lan bcur bskor te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa bstan
81a2(phal chen): nas/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po bskul ba byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad rab tu bskyod nas/ ngan song gi rgyud thams cad kyi skye ba dang / shi 'pho ba
81a3(phal chen): rab tu zhi bar byas te/ bdud kyi khyim thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgyas so/ /rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i gdan bstan pa byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi
81a4(phal chen): 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par bkod pa/ 'byam klas pa rab tu bstan nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs par 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus
81a5(phal chen): par rgyas par khyab par byas nas phyir 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la g.yas phyogs nas bskor nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs
81a6(phal chen): su byung ba'i dpal gyi spyi bor nub po/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dag thams cad ngo mtshar cher 'dzin cing / dga' ba thob par gyur te/ 'od gzer gyi dra ba snang ba 'di lta bu byung bas na chos chen po
81a7(phal chen): brjod par ni 'gyur du nges so snyam nas/ rtog pa'i blo dang ba thob par gyur to/ /'od gzer de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyi lus la thim
81a8(phal chen): par gyur ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal pad mo'i stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar
81b1(phal chen): nas/ pad mo'i snying po nges la pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga btsugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der thal mos btud te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'du shes dang ldan pa'i yid la byed pas/ de bzhin
81b2(phal chen): gshegs pa la tshigs su bcad de gsol pa/ /rnam dag blo mnga' yon tan mkhyen pas 'phags pa/ /spyod yul chags pa med pa'i pha rol phyin brnyes/ /dus gsum mnyam pa'i chos nyid
81b3(phal chen): mnyam ston pa/ /khyod la bdag ni sti stang rim gro bgyid do/ /mtshan nyid med pa'i spyod yul pha rol phyin brnyes/ /mtshan gyis shin tu bstan pa'i 'od ston mdzad/ /dri med 'od chen 'od gzer
81b4(phal chen): stong dang ldan 'gyed pa/ /bdud kyi sde rnams ma lus rab tu 'jom mdzad pa/ /phyogs bcu kun na gang rnams ji snyed mchis pa yi/ /zhing rnams thams cad ma lus rab tu skyod kyang / /thugs rje ldan pas
81b5(phal chen): su la 'ang 'jigs par myi mdzad/ /khyod kyi rdzu 'phrul mthu ni de 'dra de tshul/ /nam mkha'i dbyings la mnyam pa nyid du rab bzhugs/ /de bzhin chos dbyings mnyam pa nyid kyang brnyes gyur/ /sems can stong
81b6(phal chen): phrag bye ba grol bar mdzad cing / /sems can kun kyi sdig chen rab tu zhi mdzad/ /bskal pa stong du brtul zhugs dam po spyad de/ /byang chub mchog gi lam ni yang dag bsgrubs nas/ /chags pa med pa'i ye shes
81b7(phal chen): spyod yul 'di brnyes/ /sangs rgyas kun dang rang bzhin gcig tu rab gyur/ /rnam par 'dren pa khyod kyis 'di nas 'di bkye/ /'jig rten thams cad ma lus kun tu bskyod nas/ /cho 'phrul mtha' yas
81b8(phal chen): yang dag bstan par bgyis te/ /bdag gi lus 'dir de dag ma lus zhugs gyur/ /de la bdag gi blo gros 'di ltar skyes te/ /chos rje khyod la bdag gis zhu ba'i dus bab/ /shin tu nges pa'i chos la rab tu
82a1(phal chen): bslabs pa yi/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyang 'dus par gyur snyam/ /tshogs 'di dag pa 'dus pas rnam par dag pa/ /'jig rten slob dpon mgon pos rab tu bsngags pa/ /
82a2(phal chen): ye shes mtha' yas ldan pa yul la chags pa myed/ /de 'dra'i mthu chen dpa' bo 'di dag 'dir phyin/ /de'i don 'jig rten slob dpon drang srong chen po/ /ye shes stobs dang brtson 'grus mtha' yas
82a3(phal chen): byung gyur/ /byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag snang bar mdzad gsol/ /chos rab bdag gis gang zhus de yang bshad gsol/ /drang srong chen po'i spyod yul 'di dag bstan cing / /yang dag ma nor brjod par
82a4(phal chen): nus pa gang lags/ /skyes bu khyu mchog rnams kyi sras ni gang lags/ /'jig rten mgon gyi gtso bo khyod kyis bshad gsol/ /tshigs su bcad pa de dag gsol ma thag tu/ de'i tshe bcom ldan
82a5(phal chen): 'das kyi zhal gyi sgo nas myi bsnyengs pa'i mthar phyin pa zhes bya ba'i 'od gzer 'khor kyi 'od gzer khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa dang ldan pa byung ste/ des 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams
82a6(phal chen): cad ma lus par snang bar byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams nas g.yas phyogs su lan bcur bskor te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba stan nas/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig
82a7(phal chen): brgya stong mang po bskal pa byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad rab tu bskyod nas/ ngan song gi rgyud thams cad kyi skye ba dang / shi 'pho ba rab tu zhi bar byas te/ bdud kyi khyim thams
82a8(phal chen): cad zil gyis mnan nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bas/ rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i gdan bstan pa byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor rnams bkod pa
82b1(phal chen): 'byam klas pa rab tu bstan nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs par 'byam klas pa/ thams cad ma lus par khyab par byas nas phyir 'ongs te/
82b2(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la g.yas phyogs nas bskor nas/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i kha'i sgor nub po/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od gzer des
82b3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la reg par gyur ma thag tu de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i lus kyi seng ge'i khri/ sngon
82b4(phal chen): ci 'dra ba de las byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi seng ge'i khri brgya phrag stong gyur tu bzang zhing / khyad par du 'phags par 'dug ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i seng ge'i gdan ma gtogs par byang chub
82b5(phal chen): sems dpa' gzhan gyi lus gyi seng ge'i khri las byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i lus kyi seng ge'i khri brgya phrag stong gyur du bzang zhing khyad par du 'phags par snang ngo / /de nas byang chub
82b6(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras
82b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pas cho 'phrul chen po 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par dka' ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams rab tu dga' bar 'gyur ba bsam gyis myi khyab pa 'di lta bu bstan
82b8(phal chen): na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de gang gi sngon gyi mtshan mar 'gyur/ de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang pos/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
83a1(phal chen): chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de ni snyam du sems te/ sngon gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi cho
83a2(phal chen): 'phrul chen po 'di 'dra ba dag kyang mthong ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba bstan pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs bstan par dgongs pa dang / cho 'phrul chen po'i
83a3(phal chen): rnam pa 'di lta bu dag ston pa mdzad do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba bstan pa'i chos
83a4(phal chen): kyi rnam grangs gyi ming thos par gyur ma thag tu/ de'i tshe sa chen g.yos par gyur to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/
83a5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras legs par spobs par mdzod cig /ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
83a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye ba 'byung ba bstan pa khong du chud par byed/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'khor 'dus pa 'di ni shin tu dag pa ste/ byang chub sems
83a7(phal chen): dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong kun nas 'dus pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sngon sbyangs pa shin tu spyad pa/ las kyi mtha' shin tu sbyangs pa/ dran pa dang
83a8(phal chen): blo gros dang / rig pas shin tu 'phags pa/ rgya chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa/ mchog thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul dang / spyod pa dang tshul la rab tu gnas pa/ sangs rgyas
83b1(phal chen): kyi rjes su song ba'i 'du shes yid la byed pa ma nyams pa/ snying rje chen pos 'gro ba thams cad la rnam par blta ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa chen pos rnam par rol pa'i spyod yul
83b2(phal chen): can/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin rang gi rgyud du len pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi dpal gyi byin gyis brlabs pa ste/ de dag las stsogs pa yon tan dang legs pa tshad med
83b3(phal chen): pa mang po dang ldan pa sha stag 'ongs shing 'dus pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod kyang sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po bsnyen bkur ba/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa'i mchog tu
83b4(phal chen): phyin pa/ ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgo thams cad kyis rnam par rol par mngon par mkhas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i gnas su chud pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos
83b5(phal chen): thams cad la the tsom yongs su bcad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis byin tu brlabs pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dbang po la mkhas pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams
83b6(phal chen): cad kyi mos pa dang rnam par grol ba'i lam yang dag par ston pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs dang / rgyud yang dag par 'byung ba'i ye shes dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad
83b7(phal chen): bstan pa la pha rol phyin pa'i mchog thob pa de dag la stsogs pa yon tan mang po tshad med pa'i khyad par kyi mthar thug pa yin gyis/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
83b8(phal chen): rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye ba 'byung ba bstan pa dang / sku yang dag par bstan pa dang / dbyangs rab tu brjod pa dang thugs kyi mthu dang / yul gyi gnas dang / spyod yul bstan pa dang /
84a1(phal chen): mngon par byang chub pa'i gnas dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mngon par bsgrub pa dang / yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
84a2(phal chen): mthong zhing thos pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'grogs pas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'byung ba bstan pa la legs par spobs par mdzod cig /de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de
84a3(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/ don 'di nyid yang bslas brjod pa'i phyir/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ /
84a4(phal chen): chags myed blo gros shin tu rnam par sangs rgyas blo ldan/ /ye shes mtha' yas yul la mnyam pa nyid du gyur pa/ /rgyal ba'i spyod yul tshad med legs par yang dag shod cig /de thos sangs rgyas
84a5(phal chen): sras rnams thams cad rab tu dga' 'gyur/ /rgyal ba mchog rnams 'byung ba ji ltar byang chub sems dpas/ /khong du chud bya ji ltar de dag yang dag blta bya/ /de bzhin gshegs thugs ji 'dra sku dang
84a6(phal chen): dbyangs dang ci 'dra/ /skyes bu khyu mchog rnams kyi yul dang spyod yul ci 'dra/ /de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub ji ltar rnam par 'tshang rgya/ /chos kyi 'khor lo dam pa rgyal ba ji ltar ston mdzad/ /bde
84a7(phal chen): gshegs mya ngan 'das pa'i yang dag nyid kyang gsung ste/ /sangs rgyas sras po mtha' yas 'di dag dga' bar mdzod cig /gang gis bde gshegs chos rgyal chen po mthong bar gyur cing / /gang rnams
84a8(phal chen): 'grogs shing dge ba yang dag bskyed par byed pa/ /de dag bsod nams 'phel ba yang ma nor brjod par mdzod cig /bde gshegs mthong na jir 'gyur de dang 'grogs na jir 'gyur/ /bde gshegs
84b1(phal chen): mya ngan 'das dang 'on tam bzhugs kyang rung ste/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rnams gang gis thos par gyur cing / /yon tan 'byung gnas rnams la gang rnams dad pa bskyed pa/ /de dag don kyang
84b2(phal chen): cir 'gyur 'khor 'dir bstan par mdzod cig / byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag thams cad thal mo sbyar cing / /bde bar gshegs dang khyod dang bdag la kun kyang blta 'dod/ /dris pa 'di dag
84b3(phal chen): sems can dag pa khyod kyis lung ston/ /yon tan rgya mtsho che mnga' rnams kyi spyod yul bstan mdzod/ /de dag shin tu chos rab ldan pa'i gsung mchog brjod cing / /mkha' 'dra khyod kyis skye bo
84b4(phal chen): rnams kyi the tsom gcad mdzod/ /dpe dang rgyur ldan tshig gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs ston/ /thos nas sems can khrag khrig byang chub mchog tu sems skyed/ /ji ltar zhing rnams thams cad
84b5(phal chen): ma lus rgyas par bkang zhing / /rgyal ba'i sku yi yan lag sna tshogs yang dag ston mdzod/ /ji ltar khrag khrig chos dang ldan pa'i gsung rab brjod pa/ /sangs rgyas byang chub dpe dang rgyu yis bstan
84b6(phal chen): mdzod/ /gang zhig phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams khrag khrig thams cad kun tu/ /bskal pa mang po bye ba mtha' yas bgrangs bar song yang / /de ring rgyal sras 'dir tshogs 'di 'khor dad dang 'dra ba/ /
84b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis mthong bar shin tu dka' bas/ /de bas rgyal sras rang bzhin dag pa khyod kyis bshad mdzod/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi rigs yangs yongs su ston cing / /
84b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag thams cad thal mo sbyar te/ /yangs pa'i chos kyis sgom zhing chos la don gnyer gnas so/ /de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
85a1(phal chen): po kun tu bzang pos/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal la dmyigs nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs thams cad
85a2(phal chen): la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas skye ba 'byung ba bstan pa/ tshad med pa'i chos kyis 'byung ba 'di ni bsam gyis myi
85a3(phal chen): khyab pa'i gnas te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye ba 'byung ba ni/ rgyu gcig ma yin pa dang / rkyen gcig ma yin pas
85a4(phal chen): yang dag par 'grub bo/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag chos bcu po 'di dag la stsogs pa chos rnam pa tha dad pa brgya stong tshad med grangs med pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i tshul yang dag par
85a5(phal chen): bsgrubs pa'i rgyus de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sngon 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyabs pa'i sems dang / byang chub kyi sems tshad med pa bskyed pa
85a6(phal chen): yang dag par bsgrubs pa dang / bsam pa dang lhag pa'i bsam pa sngon shin tu sbyangs shing yang dag par bsgrubs pa dang / byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po tshad myed pas sems can yongs su
85a7(phal chen): skyabs pa dang / yang dag par bsgrub pa dang bskyod pa dang / smon lam tshad med pa rgyun chad pa med par yang dag par bsgrubs pa dang / bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs chen pos mi ngoms par yang
85a8(phal chen): dag par bsgrubs pa dang / sangs rgyas mchod cing rim gro bya ba dang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i rgyun tshad med pa yang dag par bsgrubs pa dang / thabs dang shes rab kyi lam rnam par dag cing /
85b1(phal chen): tshad med pa yang dag par bsgrubs pa dang / yon tan rnam par dag pa'i rnam pa tshad myed pa yang dag par bsgrubs pa dang / lam gyi yan lag rnam par bkod pa tshad med pa'i ye shes yang dag par
85b2(phal chen): bo sgrubs pa dang / don dang ldan pa'i chos tshad med pa khong du chud pas/ mthar phyin par bya ba yang dag par bsgrubs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po 'di dag la stsogs pa/ chos rnam pa tha dad pa
85b3(phal chen): brgya stong tshad myed grangs med pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i tshul yang dag par bsgrubs pa'i rgyus de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste dper na/ stong
85b4(phal chen): gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'byung ba ni rgyu gcig gis 'byung ba ma yin/ rkyen gcig gis 'byung ba ma yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi
85b5(phal chen): khams ni rgyu tshad med pa dang / rkyen tshad myed pa dang / bsgrub pa tshad myed pas yongs su 'grub par 'gyur te/ 'di ltar sprin chen po'i char dus las myi 'da' bar rab tu 'bab pas kyang rgyu byas la/ rlung
85b6(phal chen): gi dkyil 'khor bzhi rgyun myi chad par ldang bas kyang rgyu byas na yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /bzhi po de dag kyang gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor yongs su 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni yongs su
85b7(phal chen): gzung ba'i phyir ldang ngo / /rlung gi dkyil 'khor yongs su skem pa zhes bya ba ni/ chu'i phung po yongs su bskam pa'i phyir ldang ngo / /rlung gi dkyil 'khor yongs su gzhog pa zhes bya ba ni gzhal med
85b8(phal chen): khang thams cad yongs su dgod pa'i phyir ldang ngo / /rlung gi dkyil 'khor rnams par dgod pa zhes bya ba ni/ sems can stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gtogs pa
86a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi rkyen du skyes pa'i las dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs dang shugs kyis/ gnas kyi rnam pa'i rgyan rnam par phye ba shin tu rnam par dbye bas stong
86a2(phal chen): gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams dbye ba'i phyir ldang ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de dag la stsogs pa'i rnam pa tshad myed pas stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams
86a3(phal chen): chos nyid rab tu thob pa'i phyir/ yongs su 'byung ba'i 'gyur ba yang 'byung ba de la 'byung bar byed pa gang yang med de/ 'byung bar 'gyur ba'ang ma yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin
86a4(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyang rgyu gcig ma yin pa dang / rkyen gcig ma yin pas 'byung bar 'gyur te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs
86a5(phal chen): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni rgyu tshad myed pa dang / rnam pa tshad myed pa dang / yang dag par bsgrub pa tshad myed pas 'byung ba ste/ 'di ltar yang dag par rdzogs
86a6(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi drung du sngon chos kyi sprin gyi char chen po bab pas rgyur byas la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi rlung gi dkyil 'khor bzhi rgyun mi chad par ldang bas kyang rgyu byas nas
86a7(phal chen): yang dag par 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /bzhi gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi rlung gi dkyil 'khor chen po dran pas yang dag par bzung zhing gzungs kyis chud myi za ba zhes
86a8(phal chen): bya ba yod de/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi chos kyi sprin chen po'i char yang dag par gzung ba'i phyir ldang ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi rlung gi dkyil 'khor chen po lhag mthong dang /
86b1(phal chen): zhi gnas kyis bsgrub pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de ni nyon mongs pa thams cad yongs su skem pa'i phyir ldang ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi rlung gi dkyil 'khor chen po yongs su bsngo ba
86b2(phal chen): la mkhas pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de ni dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su bsngo ba'i phyir ldang ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi rlung gi dkyil 'khor chen po sprul pa'i rgyan rnam par
86b3(phal chen): bkod pa rnam par 'byed cing rnam par 'god pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de ni sems can sngon yongs su smin par byas pa rnams kyi rkyen du byung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su dag pa dang / de bzhin
86b4(phal chen): gshegs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba zag pa med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyi phyir ldang ngo / /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de dag la stsogs pa'i rnam pa tshad med pa dang / yang dag par bsgrub pa tshad
86b5(phal chen): pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams chos nyid rab tu thob pa'i phyir 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de la 'byung bar byed pa 'am skye bar byed pa
86b6(phal chen): gang yang med de/ 'byung ba med pa 'ang ma yin no/ /de ltar rgyal ba'i sras dag dpe'i sgo dang pos khong du chud par bya ba 'dis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos de bzhin
86b7(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas skye ba 'byung ba khong du chud par bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag gzhan yang 'di lta ste dper na/ stong gsum gyi stong
86b8(phal chen): chen po'i 'jig rten kyi khams yongs su 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i tshe/ gcig tu stug cing tha mi dad pa zhes bya ba'i sprin chen po'i char 'bab ste/ de ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i
87a1(phal chen): yongs su grub pa'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor ma gtogs par sa'i phyogs gzhan gyis gzung ba 'am bzod par myi nus so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa

87a3(phal chen): d pa' chen po de dag nyid kyi stobs dang shugs kyis bsgrubs pa'i sems gyi rgyud ma gtogs par byang chub sems dpa' bsam pa can dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis

87a6(phal chen): gang nas kyang 'ongs pa myed la gang du yang 'gro ba myed do/ /sems can rnams kyi las kyi tshogs chen pos rab tu 'bab pa yang yod do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa

87b4(phal chen): la bltas pas myig 'khrugs par 'gyur ro/ /stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i dbang phyug chen po ni ma gtogs te/ de'i sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su sbyangs pa'i khyad par kyis/ de la chung ngu na char
87b5(phal chen): pa'i thigs kyang ma rig par mi 'bab po/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa de dag yang dag par 'byung ba'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sprin kyi char mngon par 'bab pa yang /

88a8(phal chen): char 'bab pa yod de/ de ni sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa dang lta ba'i rnam pa thams cad yongs su gcod do/ /yongs su grub pa zhes bya ba chos kyi sprin chen po'i char 'bab pa yod de/
88b1(phal chen): de ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos rin po che yongs su grub par byed do/ /rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya ba chos kyi sprin chen po'i char 'bab pa yod de/ de ni sems can thams cad kyi sems dang
88b2(phal chen): bsam pa rnam par 'byed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag khong du chud par bya ba'i sgo lnga pa 'dis kyang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang

88b4(phal chen): mod kyi de ltar rnam pa tshad myed par tha dad pa'i char rnam par phye ba 'bab po/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rje chen po'i char sprin ro gcig pa las/ de ltar tshad myed
88b5(phal chen): cing rnam pa tha dad pa'i chos kyi char sna tshogs 'bab ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa yang yongs su 'byung ngo / /chos rnam par phye ba tshad myed pa yang snang zhing yod do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag khong du
88b6(phal chen): c hud par bya ba'i sgo drug pa 'dis kyang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye ba 'byung ba khong du

88b8(phal chen): gzhal med khang yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu 'dod pa la spyod pa'i lha'i bu rnams kyi gzhal med khang yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu mi rnams kyi gnas yongasu 'grub
89a1(phal chen): par 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu de ma yin pa'i sems can lhag ma gzhan rnams kyi gnas rnam par phye ba sna tshogs 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs
89a2(phal chen): pa yang dag par 'byung ba'i tshe/ yang thog ma nyid du byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes gyi rgyud rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu rang sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gyi rgyud rnams 'byung ngo / /de'i 'og
89a3(phal chen): tu nyan thos kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i ye shes kyi rgyud rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu de ma yin pa'i sems can gzhan gyi 'dus byas kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang shes pa'i rgyud rnams 'byung bar 'gyuro/ /

89b2(phal chen): lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po dang / gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu gzhan rnams kyis kyang / bskal pa 'di la ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'di snyed cig 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes
89b3(phal chen): bya ba khong du chud do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su 'grub pa'i tshe/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor dag cing 'od gsal ba zhes bya ba ldang ste/

89b7(phal chen): brtan pa zhes bya ba ldang ste/ de ni rin po che bcu yongs su gzhog pa byed do/ /bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ seng ldeng can dang / drang srong ri dang / bdud las rgyal dang / bdud las shin tu rgyal dang /

94a6(phal chen): sems kyi skad cig yud gyis shes kyang 'gro snyed kyi/ /bskal pas thams cad zil gnon rang bzhin shes mi nus/ /ji ltar chos kyi dbyings ni kun tu mtha' yas shing / /kun yin thams cad
94a7(phal chen): ma yin myi snang gzung du myed/ /de bzhin stobs bcu mnga' ba'i spyod yul tshad myed de/ /thams cad yin kyang kun myin chos dbyings rang bzhin myin/ /de bzhin nyid ni de bzhin nyid du myi rtog zhing / kun nas
94a8(phal chen): 'byung ba myed cing nam yang nub pa myed/ /de bzhin 'jig rten kun 'das de dag spyod yul te/ /de bzhin nyid dang tshul mtshungs 'phel dang 'grib pa spangs/ /yang dag mtha' ni mtha' med mtha' la gnas
94b1(phal chen): pa ste/ /dus gsum kun dang rnam pa kun tu rnam par bral/ /de bzhin mgon po phan mdzad kun kyi spyod yul te/ /dus gsum rgyas mdzad rnam pa kun tu chags myi mnga'/ /rang bzhin byas pa med pas rnam
94b2(phal chen): par 'gyur ba med/ /rang bzhin mkha' 'dra dri myed nyon mongs myed pa ste/ /de bzhin rgyal ba rnams kyi rang bzhin kun tu dag /rang bzhin 'gyur dang bral zhing yod dang med pa myin/ /sgra dang tshig las rnam
94b3(phal chen): grol dbyings rnams thams cad myed/ /'gro dang 'ong rgyal rnam rtog myed pas mya ngan 'das/ /de bzhin stobs bcu mnga' ba'i spyod yul rang bzhin myed/ /tshig gi rang bzhin kun gyis brjod par myi

94b5(phal chen): kyi cho 'phrul ci 'dra ltos/ /rgyal ba'i spyod yul 'di la 'jug par su 'dod pa/ /des ni nam mkha' 'dra ba bsam pa yongs su spongs/ /rtog dang rnam par rtog dang 'du shes 'dzin spangs te/ /nam mkha' lta
94b6(phal chen): bu'i yid kyis de la 'jug par gyis/ /de bas bde gshegs sras rnams mgon po'i spyod yul rnams/ /bdag gis dpe tsam chung shas bshad kyis mnyan par gyis/ /stobs bcu mnga' ba'i yon tan mthar
94b7(phal chen): phyin myi nus kyang / /shas tsam shes par bya ba'i don du chung zad brjod/ /de dag sku yi phrin las ji ltar 'byung ba dang / /mgon po rnams kyi gsung dang thugs kyi spyod yul dang / /stobs bcu rnams kyi yul dang
94b8(phal chen): 'khor lo bskor ba dang / /mya ngan 'da' dang dge rtsa thams cad bshad kyis nyon/ /'jig rten 'di dag ma lus skye zhing 'byung ba'i tshe/ /de la rgyu yi rnam grangs gcig ces bgrang myed kyi/ /rgyu dang tshul gyi rnam pa
95a1(phal chen): khrag khrig brgya mang gyis/ /'jig rten stong gsum kun nas gnas pa'i grangs su 'gro/ /de bzhin skyes bu'i mchog rnams skye bar 'gyur ba'i tshe/ /de dag yon tan 'di snyed yin zhes bgrang ba myed/ /
95a2(phal chen): rdul dang rdul phran bgrang nus sems can kun bsam nus/ /stobs bcu mnga' ba rnams kyi 'byung ba rnams la min/ /ji ltar sprin dang dus kyi char la rten byas shing / /char chen 'bebs byed rlung rnams bzhi
95a3(phal chen): po de bzhin te/ /dge rtsa kun dang byang chub sems dpa'i mthus/ /'jig rten stong gsum kun nas gnas pa'i grangs su 'gro/ /de bzhin stobs bcu rnams kyi chos sprin rgyur byas shing / /bsam pa rnam
95a4(phal chen): dag byed pa'i ye shes rlung ldang ste/ /sngon gyi dge ba rkyen skyes rigs par yongs bsngos pas/ /stobs bcu mgon po rnams ni 'byung zhing skye bar 'gyur/ /steng gi mkha'i dbyings las sprin chen char
95a5(phal chen): blugs pa/ /stong gsum stong chen 'jig rten kun nas 'jig 'gyur tshe/ /mkha' dbyings rgya chen dag pa'i rlung langs ma gtogs par/ /sa phyogs gzhan gyis bzod cing gzung bar mi nus so/ /de

95a7(phal chen): gzhan gyis 'dzin mi nus/ /nam mkha'i dbyings las sprin chen char pa 'bab gyur pa/ /de la 'gro dang 'ong ba nam yang yod min pa/ /de la byed pa myed de tshor ba po yang myed/ /de dag chos nyid thob 'byung rnam
95a8(phal chen): pa gzhan gyis myin/ /de bzhin stobs bcu mnga' ba'i chos sprin char 'bab pa/ /de dag 'pho dang 'ong ba yod pa ma yin yang / /byang chub sems dpa'i mthu dang legs par spyad pa'i rgyus/ /byang chub
95b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i chos kyi rang bzhin sprin kyang 'byung / /sprin gyi char bkye char thigs yongs su bgrang nus pa'i/ /sems can de 'dra khams gsum 'di na yod pa myin/ /stong gsum dbang po'i dbang phyug de ni
95b2(phal chen): ma gtogs te/ /dbang sgyur de ni sngon gyi smon lam 'bras bus bgrang / /de bzhin bde gshegs char chen 'bab pa ma lus par/ /sems can kun gyis bgrang bas gzhal bar sla ba myin/ /'jig rten
95b3(phal chen): kun na 'gro ba'i mchog gyur dbang phyug rnams/ /de dag sprin chen char chen rin chen lag bkod blta/ /rab tu zhi byed zhi byed 'byung bar byed/ /gzhan yang yongs su gcod pa de ni yongs su gcod/ /bsgrub
95b4(phal chen): pa de bzhin gzhan te de ni rin chen bsgrub/ /rnam par 'byed pa stong gsum thams cad rnam par 'byed/ /stobs bcu mnga' ba'i zhing sprin nyon mongs kun zhir byed/ /'byung ba dge stong brgya grangs kun nas
95b5(phal chen): 'byung bar byed/ /yongs su gcod pa lta ba'i rnam pa yongs gcod de/ /rgyal ba'i rin chen bsgrub cing bsam pa rnam par 'byed/ /bar snang mkha' las char 'bab ji ltar ro gcig kyang / /gnas kyi
95b6(phal chen): khyad kyis yongs su 'gyur ba sna tshogs mang / /'on kyang chu la rtog med rnam par rtog pa myed/ /tha dad rnam pa 'grangs pa de dag chos nyid tshul/ /de bzhin chos kyang gcig myin tha dad ma yin te/ /ro
95b7(phal chen): gcig zhi zhing rtog med rnam par rtog med de/ /'on kyang sangs rgyas chos 'grangs mu med 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de ni rdul phran rnams kyi chos nyid tshul yin no/ /ji ltar thog mar gzugs khams
95b8(phal chen): gzhal med khang pa 'byung / /de nas 'dod khams gzhal med khang rnams rnam par 'god/ /de nas sa steng myi yi gnas rnam rnam bkod de/ /de nas klu dang dri za 'gro ba kun kyi gnas/ /de bzhin stobs
96a1(phal chen): bcu mnga' ba de dag 'byung ba'i tshe/ /thog mar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mu med 'byung / /de nas zhi dga' rang rgyal theg la gnas pa rnams/ /de nas dbang du gyur pa'i de nas 'gro kun
96a2(phal chen): gyi/ /ji ltar pad mo sangs rgyas skye ba'i ltas gyur pas/ /sngon chad sangs rgyas mthong ba'i lha rnams dgar 'gyur zhing / /chu las brten cing 'od gsal gzhal myed khang yang 'byung / /rlung las 'jig
96a3(phal chen): rten ris ris cha char 'god pa byed/ /sangs rgyas sngon gyi dge ba'i 'od gsal ltas yin te/ /des ni sangs rgyas rgyal sras kun kyi thugs chud 'gyur/ /ye shes yongs dag dkyil 'khor mkha'

96a5(phal chen): gel ba'i sman gyi gnas yin te/ /mkha' la gnas su bya ba gang yang myed pa yin/ /mgon po rnams kyang shes rab ye shes bzhi la bzhugs/ /ye shes thugs rje byams pa thabs kyis yongs su gzung / /
96a6(phal chen): rgyal ba'i chos rnams ji snyed de dag rnams su 'dus/ /rdul myed shes rab de ni gnas med lus kyang myed/ /'jig rten byung nas tshad myed mang po kun kyang 'tsho/ /sa la gnas dang chu la gnas pa
96a7(phal chen): thams cad dang / /nam mkha'i lha dang sa steng gzhal med khang la gnas pa dang / /rkang gnyis rkang bzhi sems can thams cad nye bar 'tsho/ /de bzhin skyes mchog dbang po chos kyi rgyal skyes pa/ /

96b1(phal chen): pas 'jig rten mgo rmongs 'gyur/ /'on kyang 'gro la phan don sems can shes bya'i phyir/ /myi mkhas 'gro ba bstan phyir ye shes bstan don du/ /rgyal ba rnams kyi don rab dpe myed dpes

96b3(phal chen): pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos

97a1(phal chen): gnas thams cad du khyab pa yin yang / gang du 'ong ba med cing rjes su song ba med par shes par bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni nam mkha' la gzugs myed pa'i phyir ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i

97b8(phal chen): ba'i las yongs su bskyed cing sdig pa'i las rnam par bzlog pas kyang nye bar 'tsho ba yin/ shes rab kyi 'od snang bar mdzad cing gti mug gi mun pa rnam par sel bas kyang nye bar 'tsho ba yin/

98a8(phal chen): ma nyid du ri'i rgyal po 'di lta ste/ ri rab ri'i rgyal po la snang bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og du de ma yin pa'i ri chen po gzhan la snang bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu ri nag po dag la 'ang snang bar 'gyur ro/ /
98b1(phal chen): de'i 'og tu sa phyogs mthon po rnams su snang bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu 'dzam bu'i gling 'di'i phyogs dma' ba dag kyang snang bar byed de/ 'on kyang nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la 'dir ni thog ma nyid du

98b3(phal chen): mthon dman gyi khyad par gyis mtho mtho la sngar 'char ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes kyi sku che ba nyi

98b6(phal chen): ro/ /de'i 'og tu nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg par zhugs pa rnams la 'char bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu dge ba'i rtsa ba nges pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la bsam pa'i snod ji
98b7(phal chen): lta ba bzhin du ye shes kyi snang ba chen po yang dag par ston pa'i tshul gyis 'char bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu chung ngu na log par nges pa'i sems can yan chad/ sems can thams cad
98b8(phal chen): la 'ang de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi 'od gzer chen po yang dag par 'char bar 'gyur ro/ /de ltar shar nas kyang sems can rnams la shin tu phan par gyur te/ ma 'ongs pa'i rgyu yang
99a1(phal chen): yongs su smin par mdzad cing / dge ba'i chos kyis rnam par 'phel bar mdzad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi sku nyi ma'i 'od gzer de dag ni sems can 'di rnams la/
